Current Commentary

The Abruptly Deteriorating Italo-Ethiopian War

— Hua

The Italo-Ethiopian War, having lasted for over five months, has recently shown signs of an abrupt downturn. Since the battle of Amba Aradam at the beginning of last month, the Ethiopian army, despite its brave attacks, suffered heavy losses and was forced to retreat. Subsequently, the Italian army advanced rapidly northward, capturing Gondar and moving westward to the Lake Tana area. They then concentrated their forces southward, seizing Dessie, a crucial stronghold leading to the Ethiopian capital. Simultaneously, in the southern Ethiopian Ogaden region, the Italian forces led by Graziani also advanced with full force, aiming to occupy Harar and Jijiga in the shortest possible time. Regarding the capture of Dessie and the outcome of the battle north of Lake Ashangi, Italian and Ethiopian war reports are inconsistent. The Italian side claims a great victory and the capture of Dessie, while the Ethiopian side denies this, stating that the Ethiopian Emperor's army of 20,000 troops achieved a great victory southwest of Lake Ashangi, killing 2,400 Italian soldiers. Clearly, neither side's war reports can be fully trusted. However, generally speaking, the Italian army currently holds a distinct advantage. If they completely secure and consolidate the Dessie position, the fall of the Ethiopian capital is imminent.

However, we believe that the outcome of the Italo-Ethiopian War cannot be judged solely on the developments on the East African battlefield, but must also consider two other important aspects. Simply put, the Italo-Ethiopian War is being fought on three fronts: a military front in East Africa, a diplomatic front in Geneva, and an economic front within Italy. Therefore, in addition to the situation in East Africa, we should also observe the situation in Geneva and within Italy.

In fact, Ethiopia's failure in the Italo-Ethiopian War is mainly due to shortcomings on the Geneva diplomatic front. The implementation of sanctions against Italy has been halted to a certain extent, and the failure of Germany and Austria to participate has also undermined the sanctions front to some extent. At the same time, Hitler's tearing up of the Locarno Pact has suddenly intensified the situation in Western Europe. The differing attitudes of Britain and France towards Germany have greatly affected the anti-Italian front in Geneva. Therefore, the proposal of the Committee of Thirteen for a truce between Italy and Ethiopia ultimately failed due to Italy's firm rejection. The League of Nations could not tighten sanctions against Italy in accordance with the Covenant, and the Italian army was able to advance towards Ethiopia with all its strength, determined to force a capitulation.

However, although the Ethiopian army in East Africa failed to hold its ground consistently, and the sanctions action in Geneva could not be carried out consistently, the Italian internal economic front has suffered severely during the war. According to a Havas dispatch from Paris on the 13th of this month, Italy's gold reserves are now decreasing by 500 million lire per month. As of recently, the cost of the East African war has exceeded 70 billion lire. It is estimated that the cost of repatriating the Italian army after the end of the East African war will require huge expenditures. The total war expenses will amount to 120 billion lire. We cannot underestimate the painful lessons Italy has learned from obtaining a victory at such a high price. According to a Havas dispatch from London on the 14th, the Rome correspondent of the Daily Telegraph, Grigore, recently published an article stating, "Regardless of who wins or loses the East African war, Italy will inevitably be impoverished, and its export trade will inevitably be insignificant for at least 20 years." The impact of Italy's invasion of Ethiopia on the economic front can be seen from this. We must not ignore the impact of this blow on the internal rule of Italy.

In the current situation, we cannot yet estimate how the Italo-Ethiopian War will end. Italy's hope is, of course, to take advantage of the weakness on the Geneva diplomatic front to intensify its victory on the East African military front in order to conceal its failure on the domestic economic front. However, judging from the Ethiopian Emperor's resolute stance, it is difficult to say whether Italy's hope will be as smooth as desired. On the Ethiopian side, all the weak and small nations of the world, and those who sympathize with them, will give the assessment of "glorious even in defeat."

Gu Weijun to Arrive in Paris Tomorrow

(Paris) Dr. Gu Weijun, the Chinese Ambassador, and his wife have landed at the port of Genoa in Italy and are traveling to France by train. They are scheduled to arrive here at 8:10 am on the 1st of next week. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

Ship Carrying Chinese Antiquities Still Escorted to Shanghai by British Warships

Gibraltar The British company's ship, the Ranpura, which ran aground in Gibraltar for two days, was refloated last night. Tonight, it will continue its journey to Marseille, carrying undamaged Chinese antiquities. A British destroyer will accompany it along the way for protection. After confirming that the ship's hull was undamaged, it was ordered to continue its voyage to the Far East. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

Chinese Art Exhibition at the London Museum Features 2,500 Exquisite Treasures

(London) The collection of Chinese art by Mr. Omorphopoulos was exhibited today at the Victoria and Albert Museum. The opening ceremony was officiated by the Chinese Ambassador, Guo Taiqi. After Ambassador Guo arrived, he was introduced to the guests by Mr. Bellham, a permanent official of the Ministry of Education. Ambassador Guo gave a speech, saying that Mr. Omorphopoulos's talent in collecting such exquisite and unparalleled works of art was truly admirable. The famous poet, writer, speaker, Mr. Ping Rong, also gave a speech. Mr. Omorphopoulos's exhibition features a total of 2,500 works of art, of which only 200 were displayed at the recent Burlington House Chinese Art Exhibition. Mr. Omorphopoulos has now sold his entire collection to the country at a low price. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

(London) A man named Omorphopoulos, a famous collector, has a magnificent collection of Chinese art. It was publicly exhibited today at the Victoria Museum, with the opening ceremony officiated by the Chinese Ambassador, Guo Taiqi. He delivered a speech, saying, "The exhibitions held by several governments are often fleeting and cannot last for long. After the public exhibition of Chinese art at Burlington Palace recently, this grand event is being held again. Not only do they reflect each other, but they also make the memory of the last exhibition last for a long time. Now, the various treasures of the country are on their way back home. Although they are not displayed here, Mr. Omorphopoulos's collection can replace them without shame, because its variety is vast, exquisite, and unparalleled, enough to represent the artistic genius of China. It is truly commendable that a person has devoted his life to collecting so many treasures, making him famous throughout the world." Ambassador Guo also said, "What is beautiful is true, and what is true is beautiful. This is a timeless truth that cannot be erased. This is all we know and always know. Political policies are sometimes exhausted, party conflicts may continue to exist, but this saying alone can transcend any dispute, reaching far and wide. This is the only thing that we can take comfort in," he said. (Havas dispatch, 17th)

Germany Establishes Chinese Society New Address to Open on June 13th

Frankfurt The Chinese Society has worked hard over the past ten years, and its new headquarters are scheduled to open on June 13th. The new Chinese Ambassador, Cheng Tianfang, and prominent German figures will participate in this grand ceremony. The president of the society, Dr. Rossel, will deliver a welcome speech. Experts will present scientific papers and scholars will give lectures on that day. The opening program will be divided into three days. After the opening ceremony, the new headquarters of the Chinese Society will be open to the public, welcoming visitors from all walks of life. The society has collected many treasures that are not available in other museums, it is said. (National News Agency dispatch, 17th)

No Anti-Chinese Sentiment in the Philippines

(Manila) The staff of the Chinese Consulate here have not heard of any news of anti-Chinese sentiment among Filipinos. Nanjing is very uneasy about this. The Chinese Vice-Consul recently told a reporter from the Associated Press that he had not heard of any anti-Chinese movement in the Philippines. Several Chinese have died in various places since January, but they were all small merchants killed by bandits. Occasional incidents of personal animosity do occur, but they cannot be regarded as anti-Chinese, he said. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Italian Troops Besiege South Manchuria Railway Station Three Japanese Station Staff Killed Sixty-Five Japanese Soldiers' Ashes Return Home

Only about 700 foreign guests and prominent officials will be invited to a banquet to celebrate on that day, it is said. (Hualian News Agency dispatch, 18th)

(Domei News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Third Trial of Japanese Corruption Case Former Railway Minister Ogawa Sentenced to Two Years' Imprisonment and a Fine of 192,120 Yuan

(Nanjing) The appeal trial of the five private railway corruption cases of former Railway Minister Ogawa Heikichi opened at 1:40 pm on the 18th. Prosecutor Takeshi Matsuoka argued that the defendants in this case were mostly prominent figures in political and financial circles, and the amount of bribes received and given was also huge. Therefore, from a legal perspective, it was a major case. The facts of the crime were the same as in the second trial and should be found guilty. The prosecutor then refuted the defendant's arguments, pointing out the facts of the crime for two hours. Finally, he requested a sentence of two years' imprisonment and a fine of 192,120 yuan for Ogawa, and the same as before for the other six defendants. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Amidst Sino-US Negotiations, Silver Prices Soar in the London Market Total Purchases Reach 20 Million Ounces Britain Suspicious of Our Restoration of the Silver Standard

(London) Speculators here, encouraged by the hope of current Sino-US silver issue talks, purchased silver bars today, so spot prices rose 1/8 of a penny, and forward prices rose 1/16. It is estimated today that India purchased a total of 3 million ounces of silver. It is widely believed that the Chinese government is now the main purchaser, and it is estimated that speculators have purchased between 15 million and 20 million ounces. Except for some that have actually been shipped to India, it is generally believed that there are not many real purchasers. Since speculators' demand has been met by genuine sales, the position of the bulls is difficult to maintain for long. Those in charge are very suspicious of the possibility that the outcome of the Sino-US talks could enable China to restore the silver standard at the current prices. This is because China would have to pay 17.5 pence per ounce to repurchase the silver it needs. (Reuters dispatch, 18th)

(Paris) A correspondent from the Economic and Financial Communications Agency stationed in New York recently announced that after talks between Chen Guangfu, the general manager of the Shanghai Commercial and Savings Bank of China, and the US authorities, a tripartite agreement has been reached between China, the United States, and Britain, stipulating that Britain and the United States will jointly assist China in maintaining its currency system and helping China solve complex monetary problems. According to well-informed sources, the method is that the United States will continue to purchase silver from China at a price higher than the international market price, so that China can obtain US dollars and gold to adjust foreign exchange rates. However, China must not sell its silver to other buyers in order to prevent fluctuations in the silver market. In Britain, it is planned to lend funds to China so that Chinese banks can increase their foreign exchange reserves. Even if there is a need to sell silver dollars commercially or financially, the injection of pounds will prevent fluctuations. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

(Washington) It was heard here today from those in charge that the rise in silver prices in London and New York does not affect the US Treasury Department's silver purchase program. The price increase was caused by speculation in London and Mumbai. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

(Washington) Chen Guangfu, the leader of the Chinese banking group, will attend the grand banquet of the Gridiron Club, held here every six months, on Saturday. The Chinese Ambassador to the United States, Shi Zhaoji, will also attend the banquet. According to the club, foreigners are not usually invited to this kind of banquet, so Chen's invitation is a special honor. (National News Agency dispatch, 17th)

Li Wenfan Discusses Provisional Clauses of the Draft Constitution Meeting of the Central Draft Constitution Review Committee

(Nanjing) Li Wenfan said that the constitution is the fundamental law of the country, and it is of great importance to the future of the country and the welfare of the people. The draft constitution has been worked on by the Legislative Yuan for more than four years and has been reviewed by the central government many times. The content is quite substantial and detailed. Committee Member Ye Chucang went to Hong Kong last year on behalf of the central government to welcome Mr. Hu Guomian home and also discussed the content of the draft constitution. Recently, he exchanged views with Central Committee member Wang Liangchou in Shanghai. The proposed provisional clauses to be added by various parties are to meet actual needs and are equivalent to the implementing rules in a regulation. The Review Committee will probably complete the review of the entire draft constitution today and submit it to the Central Temporary Standing Committee next Monday for approval in principle. It will then be sent to the Legislative Yuan for revisions and amendments to the clauses, with the aim of publishing it as scheduled on May 5th. (Special dispatch, 18th)

(Nanjing) The Central Draft Constitution Review Committee held a meeting at 3:00 pm on the 18th. More than ten people attended, including Ye Chucang, Li Wenfan, Zhou Fohai, Wang Luyi, Shao Yuanchong, Wu Jingxiong, Wang Shijie, and Wang Yongbin. The meeting was adjourned at 6:00 pm, presided over by Ye Zhongxi. It is said that a review opinion will be formulated and submitted to the Central Standing Committee for a decision. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Chen Juesheng, Lin Shize, etc. Discuss Anti-Smuggling Measures

(Tianjin) Chen Juesheng, Lin Shize, and the Chief Inspector of Customs, Mr. Halliwell, discussed concrete cooperative measures for anti-smuggling in North China this morning. The new anti-smuggling order from the Ministry of Finance is expected to arrive in Tianjin before the 25th, and all relevant parties are preparing to promulgate it after receiving it. (Special dispatch, 18th)

(Nanjing) Smuggling of goods into North China has not decreased slightly, and the smuggling of edible salt out of North China is also extremely rampant. These smugglers are mostly salt smugglers, who originally used small boats and sampans to transport goods secretly for sale to Japan. Now the organization has gradually expanded, and some have also switched to using motorboats or small wheels for towing. The North China Anti-Smuggling Team has stepped up its prevention efforts, but because they come and go unpredictably, it is not easy to completely eliminate them for a while. It has been found that a portion of the customs revenue from salt is provided for indemnity payments and foreign debt guarantees. Since the September 18th Incident, the customs of Northeast China have been seized, and the guarantee has been completely increased on the existing customs. If smuggling is not stopped, customs revenue will not only be directly affected by tax evasion, but also indirectly affected by the reduction in legitimate imports. If this continues, problems will inevitably arise with the guarantee, which is of great importance to the interests of various countries and China's national credit. The Chief Inspector of Customs is quite anxious. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Guan Linzheng telegraphed on the 17th, stating that our vanguard had arrived at Pitiaowan, east of Wucheng Township, which belongs to Xian County, at noon today, and encountered the false First Army Corps, the 1st and 2nd Divisions from the south, and a group of more than 1,000 bandits who came from there. We immediately launched a head-on attack. The bandits launched a fierce assault on us five or six times. Our troops concentrated their firepower and fired fiercely with machine guns. After the cabinet received the telegram, it sent a telegram of commendation. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Tongpei and Feng Three Counties Repair Dikes in Sections Floods in Suqian Cause Disaster Again

(Xuzhou) The disaster-stricken areas north of Xuzhou are working to restore the Wei Lake Dike. A Huangzai Relief and Reconstruction Engineering Office has now been organized to take charge. Commissioner Shao is the director, and the magistrates of Tongpei and Feng counties are the deputy directors. The dikes of the three counties are divided into four sections for separate blocking and repair. There is no problem. However, dredging the Bulao River to guide the water downstream is still being planned. (Special dispatch, 18th)

(Xuzhou) It was reported from Suqian that the water in the Luoma and Huangdun lakes in Suqian rose after the water levels fell last winter, and wheat seeds were sown in the lake fields. Heavy rains a few days ago caused the water levels to rise and submerge the fields. Suqian telegraphed Xuzhou yesterday to report the disaster. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Ninth Anniversary of Establishing the Capital in Nanjing: National Government Held Commemorative Meeting Yesterday; Chairman Lin Speaks on Efforts to Build the Capital; Tour of the Newly Completed National Government Building

(Nanjing) The National Government held a commemorative meeting at 10:00 AM on the 18th to celebrate the ninth anniversary of establishing the capital in Nanjing. Attendees included Feng Yuxiang, Ye Chucang, Zhang Ji, Deng Jiayan, Huang Fusheng, He Yingqin, Chen Diaoyuan, Zhang Zhijiang, Jiang Zuobin, Huang Musong, Shi Ying, Wang Yongbin, Chen Shuren, Zhang Yipeng, Chen Xunyong, Jiao Yitang, Yu Feipeng, Li Wenfan, Wang Qi, Zhang Mojun, Wang Gupan, Chen Qicai, Lü Chao, Wei Huai, and other senior civil and military officials from the National Government and various ministries and departments, totaling over 600 people. After the music was played, Chairman Lin led the attendees in performing the ceremony and delivered a speech. He began by stating that today was the ninth anniversary of the National Government establishing the capital in Nanjing, recalling that the National Government was established in Guangzhou on July 1, 1925. On July 15, 1926, in accordance with the late Premier's will, the Northern Expedition was launched. By September of the same year, the National Revolutionary Army's forces had advanced to the Yangtze River basin. After the Chinese Nationalist Party's purge nine years ago today, the capital was established in Nanjing. At that time, the Northern Government had not yet fallen, the Yellow River basin had not yet been recovered, and the remaining enemy forces continued to shell across the river. Amidst the booming cannons, the National Government faced difficulties and worked hard to build the nation. By 1928, the warlords were eliminated, the country was unified, the military period ended, the five-yuan system was created, and political tutelage was implemented. Time flies, and it has already been nine years. Recalling this day last year, we held the eighth anniversary commemoration here, hoping that all colleagues would revive the spirit of national construction, cooperate fully, and seek progress for the capital. Now, a full year has passed. As we reflect on the past, how many of the capital construction plans that the late Premier instructed us to implement have we achieved, and how many remain unfinished? He then explained the reasons why the late Premier designated Nanjing as the capital, stating that in the late Premier's will, the Premier's capital construction plan was profound and extensive. Its purpose was not only to make Nanjing the national political center and cultural center but also to make Nanjing the national transportation center and economic center. At the same time, it was to make it the first metropolis on the Pacific coast. The Premier wanted to take Nanjing as the capital, in addition to Nanjing being the most suitable place to establish the capital, there are other meanings, which is to make it an important town in national defense, because today China's national defense, sea defense is more important than land defense, the economic essence and cultural center of our country, Most of them are along the Yangtze River and the sea. Nanjing is located in the middle of China's coastline and at the important intersection of the Yangtze River's lower reaches and the sea. Establishing the capital here is enough to show the nation-building spirit of our nation. Thirdly, he said that the capital construction undertakings, such as water and electricity transportation, have made great progress. Most of the main roads have been completed. The population has increased from more than 200,000 to more than one million. Education, health, and various public undertakings are developing day by day. The construction of the mausoleum area is roughly scaled, and many trees have been planted. In a few years, forests will be everywhere. At the same time, the national railway lines, highways, and various transportation constructions centered on Nanjing are all making progress amidst difficult work and material shortages, making the connection between the central government and various provinces more agile than before. But compared with the Premier's plan, it is still far behind. Compared with the capitals of other countries in the world, there are still shortcomings, so we still need to work harder. At the same time, we must pay more attention to the prosperity and stability of the capital. It is not just the luck of a local part of Nanjing. Its importance has a great relationship with the prosperity and decline of China's national fortune and the peace of the Far East. If the rural areas go bankrupt and the four seas are in poverty, the capital will never be prosperous alone. If there are many incidents in the border areas and the bandits in Jin, Shaanxi, and Sichuan provinces are not suppressed, the capital will never be able to celebrate stability alone. Since ancient times, it has been said that adversity makes a nation strong. We hope that the past national disasters have reached the limit. Extremes beget opposites. We should uphold the late Premier's will, continue the spirit of establishing the capital in Nanjing in those years, work hard, and consolidate the foundation of the country. Finally, he quoted the "Tian Bao" chapter of the Book of Songs to wish the Republic of China a long life. The speech ended at 10:30 AM, and after the ceremony, the National Government officials invited the participants to visit the newly completed National Government building. The staff of the National Government's civil, military, and accounting offices also scheduled gatherings at the government in the afternoon to celebrate. (18th, Central News Agency)

Legislative Yuan Reviews Draft Law on Mediation of Rent Disputes

(Nanjing) Regarding the draft law on mediation of rent disputes, the Legislative Yuan's Legislative and Land Committees appointed three members, including Yao Chuanfa, to conduct a preliminary review. On the morning of the 18th, relevant agencies were invited to send representatives to the Yuan to hold a meeting to discuss the matter. After consultation, it was generally agreed that the drafting of the law on mediation of rent disputes took place before the implementation of the Land Law. Now that the Land Law has been implemented on March 1, the issue of setting standard house rents can be handled by citing Article 162 of the Land Law. The Civil Procedure Law also has provisions on mediation of rent disputes. It seems unnecessary to separately create a law on mediation of rent disputes. A draft review report will be submitted to the two committees for review and then to the Yuan for deliberation. (18th, Central News Agency)

Spanish General Strike Ends; State of Alert Extended for Thirty Days; 200 Fascists Arrested; Many Security Force Officers Also Apprehended

Madrid The general strike was officially declared over at midnight yesterday. Police arrested fascist leaders throughout the country. (18th, Havas)

Madrid After the General Confederation of Labor (CGT) announced a general strike, the situation in the capital remained calm. Police conducted searches of the residences of many residents and discovered that many members of the fascist organization "Falange" were privately hiding weapons. They were immediately arrested and handed over to the "Emergency Court" for processing. The cabinet recently ordered an extension of the state of alert by thirty days because the original deadline was approaching. (18th, Havas)

Madrid The government, due to the tense situation caused by the Labour Front's resistance to the Fascist Party, has resolved to extend the current state of alert by 30 days. When the Labour Front declared a 24-hour strike, demanding that the government take drastic action against the Fascist Party, a total of 225 troublemakers were arrested, including 200 Fascist Party members and the rest members of the National Guard. At the same time, many National Guard commanders have been replaced. The general strike ended at midnight. Although there were many riots, none were of a serious nature. This is sufficient proof of the strength of the far-left party and the Communist Party. The government, fearing that the general strike would be extended indefinitely, had approved many of the demands made by the extremists, including the arrest of Fascist Party members and the changing of the National Guard commanders. (18th, Reuters)

Madrid After the General Confederation of Labor announced the general strike, Vidal, secretary of the executive committee of the Socialist Party, immediately declared that the CGT had announced the strike to protest against the Fascists who took the opportunity to cause trouble during the funeral of Lieutenant Leffler of the security forces yesterday. The general strike movement may end at midnight today, he said. Furthermore, yesterday, during the funeral of Lieutenant Leffler, some officers of the security forces and the army violated the orders of the Minister of the Army and participated without permission, which was one of the reasons for the CGT's dissatisfaction. The authorities have now arrested those officers. In addition, Marol, the director of the National Investigation Team, and Levas, a senior police officer in the Police Department, were dismissed by the government for failing to maintain law and order. (17th, Havas)

Madrid After President Zamora resigned, the government has decided to convene a national electorate on the 26th of this month to elect representatives, who will then meet with members of the House of Representatives on May 10 to elect a successor to the presidency. Former Minister of the Army Robles, leader of the right-wing Popular Action Party, recently declared that members of his party do not intend to participate in the election of these representatives. (17th, Havas)

French Election Campaign: No Fewer Than 5,000 Competitors

(Paris) It was learned today that no fewer than 5,000 people are competing for the 614 seats in the Chamber of Deputies election to be held on April 26. The number of political parties in France is evident from this. However, the real competition is only between the People's Front and the National Front. The People's Front includes the Communist Party, the Socialist Party, and most of the Radical Socialist Party, while the National Front is composed of the Central Party and the Right Party. Each party now takes peace, patriotism, and prosperity as its three major banners. The difference lies in the means to achieve the above three goals. The right-wing trusts in armed forces and the power of heavy industry prosperity, while the left-wing trusts in the League of Nations, jobs for everyone, and the nationalization of industry and banking. In fact, the first round of voting may not have a decisive outcome, and a second round of voting is bound to be held on May 3. Therefore, the atmosphere is not yet tense. It is generally believed that this Chamber of Deputies election may have a slight shift to the left, and the Radical Socialist Party, which has long held a pivotal position, may have its power split by the Socialist Party and the Central Party. However, in any case, France's attitude towards major international issues will not be affected by a slight shift in power, because the French people now unanimously demand protection from unwarranted foreign attacks and the freedom to live and work in peace. (17th, Reuters)

British Budget Expenses Increased by 19 Million Pounds; National Defense Costs Still Require More Than 22 Million Pounds

(London) Next Tuesday, Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain will present the budget to the House of Commons. It is generally believed that the Chancellor does not want to make any drastic changes to the current tax base. This is further believed because the Chancellor must inform his cabinet colleagues of the contents of the budget until next Monday. Therefore, although the day of the budget presentation is approaching, the public is still indifferent to it. The large increase in national defense spending has made any major tax cuts impossible, but industry has seen great prosperity in recent years. The Chancellor will be able to raise funds for the large increase in spending from increased national tax revenue. Budget spending will reach 772 million pounds, an increase of 19 million pounds compared to last year. In addition, a supplementary national defense budget of approximately 22.2 million pounds will have to be submitted within twelve months, which will be raised by Treasury bills or the issuance of national defense bonds. According to the Chancellor's estimate last year, national income may increase by 46 million pounds. If this prediction is correct, it will not be difficult to cope with the increased national expenses without having to collect new taxes to raise these funds. (16th, Reuters)

Thirteen-Nation Committee Announces Failure of Italian-Ethiopian Mediation; Speeding up Sanctions Postponed for Discussion; League of Nations Administrative Council to Meet Tomorrow

(Geneva) The League of Nations Thirteen-Nation Committee today formally announced that the mediation of the Italian-Ethiopian dispute has failed. The committee is now unable to continue the peace talks and has decided to convene a meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council to deal with the crisis. The League of Nations Administrative Council is now scheduled to meet next Monday. (17th, National News Agency)

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee's decision that the mediation of the East African War has failed is extremely important, as the committee was entrusted by the Eighteen-Nation Committee, the full committee on sanctions against Italy, to discuss a peaceful resolution to the Italian-Ethiopian War. Now that it has admitted the failure of mediation, it must return the entrusted mandate to the Eighteen-Nation Committee, and the Eighteen-Nation Committee must now consider the sanctions against Italy under Article 16 of the League of Nations. Oil embargoes and even military plans will now be at the forefront. The Chairman of the Thirteen-Nation Committee, Madariaga, will submit his report to the Eighteen-Nation Committee today and will present it at the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting at 10:30 AM on Sunday. It is expected that this Administrative Council meeting will be very important. In addition to recording the failure of mediation, it must also consider the report of the Eighteen-Nation Committee on the progress of sanctions. The convening of the Eighteen-Nation Committee will clearly be decided by the Administrative Council. Large scale postponements until after the French general election will be in effect. (18th, Reuters)

(Geneva) It is reported that the representatives of the countries of the Thirteen-Nation Committee, including British Foreign Secretary Eden, have agreed that the convening date of the Eighteen-Nation Committee should be postponed as much as possible, even until after the French parliamentary elections (scheduled for April 26 and May 3). During this period, Vasconcelos, the chairman of the committee, will submit a written report on the current situation to the representatives of the countries participating in the committee and will appoint a committee of experts to review the effectiveness of the current sanctions. This committee of experts will meet in the middle of next week. According to this agency's reporter, the postponement of the Eighteen-Nation Committee was the result of talks between British Foreign Secretary Eden and French Minister Without Portfolio Peng Gu. (17th, Havas)

League of Nations Outside Contact, Situation More Optimistic, Thirteen-Nation Committee to Draft Report

(Geneva) After the League of Nations Administrative Council's Thirteen-Nation Committee failed to mediate the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, it decided yesterday to submit a report on the situation to the Administrative Council. The chief representatives of the countries concerned continued their activities this morning, and the situation is now more optimistic. The committee rejected yesterday all measures that could cause adverse reactions in Europe, and Britain and France are also making every effort to reach a mutual understanding. League of Nations personnel believe that this will greatly clarify the atmosphere here. According to what our correspondent has learned, the representatives of various countries discussed not only the Italo-Ethiopian dispute but also the general situation in Europe during their talks this morning, especially the Rhine issue. French Minister without Portfolio Peng Gu met with Soviet representative, i.e., the country's ambassador to France, Botanin, Romanian representative Antoniate, and Polish representative Komarnicki. Committee Chairman Madariaga, with the assistance of League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, has completed the draft of the report and will submit it to the committee for review this afternoon and then to the Administrative Council next Monday. This report is a brief account of how the committee has carried out the tasks entrusted to it by the Administrative Council (i.e., to monitor the development of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute and seek solutions at any time). The content is nothing more than three points: The Thirteen-Nation Committee sent a note to the two warring countries on March 3, inviting them to participate in peace talks. After Italy and Ethiopia accepted the invitation one after another, the Thirteen-Nation Committee met in London on March 23 and decided to entrust Madariaga to work with League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol to mediate between Italy and Ethiopia. The process and reasons for the failure of the two to talk with the representatives of the parties concerned, but the report will omit the issue of responsibility for the failure of the talks and the consequences that may arise. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee of the League of Nations Administrative Council continued its meeting this afternoon and acknowledged that the committee's reconciliation efforts to resolve the Italo-Ethiopian dispute had failed. It was also decided to submit a report on the discussions to the Administrative Council. This report will be drafted by the committee at its final meeting tomorrow and then submitted to the Administrative Council for review. According to what our correspondent has learned, the above resolution was advocated by French Minister without Portfolio Peng Gu. British Foreign Secretary Eden had previously stated that if the reconciliation efforts failed, the subsequent steps could be taken in one of two ways: either immediately convene the Eighteen-Nation Committee to discuss the issue of intensifying sanctions, or submit an application to the Administrative Council. Peng Gu's current proposal is the second method, which the Thirteen-Nation Committee has decided to follow. The Administrative Council is now scheduled to meet at 10:30 am next Monday, when Committee Chairman Madariaga will attend to report the failure publicly so that the two parties concerned, Italy and Ethiopia, can formally present their views to the Administrative Council and let world opinion judge the merits of the case. Other countries concerned can also take this opportunity to express their position. The Administrative Council will pass a resolution after the discussion is over, but it is unknown whether this resolution will only record the fact that the negotiations have failed and appeal to the two warring countries again to maintain peace, while postponing the implementation of intensified sanctions, or decide to postpone the meeting temporarily so that the governments of the countries concerned can reconsider the situation during the postponement period. According to what our correspondent has learned, although the reconciliation efforts of the Thirteen-Nation Committee have failed, the future is quite optimistic in terms of the cooperation of the member states of the League of Nations, because all countries seem to advocate that the handling of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute should be adapted to the needs of the European situation. British Foreign Secretary Eden and French Minister without Portfolio Peng Gu have recently issued statements to the press, praising each other's spirit of mutual understanding. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

(Paris) After the League of Nations Administrative Council's Thirteen-Nation Committee failed to mediate the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, well-known reporter Madame Tabouis recently published a commentary in the L'Œuvre, saying, "Although the mediation efforts of the Thirteen-Nation Committee have failed, there is one result that is still commendable. In other words, the current relationship between Britain and France has now improved, and the proposal to intensify sanctions against Italy is enough to cause friction between Britain and France. As for forcing Italy to stop the war, only military sanctions can be effective. British Foreign Secretary Eden is fully aware of all these points and should also make the British government understand them. This is the so-called result. At that time, if the British cabinet can accept this idea, the Administrative Council of the League of Nations may pass a resolution at its meeting next Monday to record the failure of the Thirteen-Nation Committee's mediation. On the contrary, if the British cabinet instructs Eden to adopt a positive policy, Eden will certainly demand that the Administrative Council of the League of Nations intensify sanctions, including the oil embargo, until a fair solution to the Italo-Ethiopian dispute is reached. However, people with good sources of information here still do not know what attitude the British cabinet will take." (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Addis Ababa The Ethiopian Emperor sent a note to the League of Nations, accusing the member states of the League of Nations of delaying the implementation of effective sanctions against Italy and demanding the immediate implementation of a plan to end the Italian aggression. This claim does not help the situation. According to Ethiopians, the latest methods are now being used to build battle lines on the three main roads. Ethiopia has recently purchased many anti-tank guns and will resist the advance of the Italian army on the southern front. However, the real crisis in Ethiopia is the attack on its rear by the Italian army on the northern front. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Issue of Restoring Military Preparations in Turkish Straits, Soviet Russia Expresses Approval in Reply

Angora It is widely rumored in Athens that Turkish troops have entered the demilitarized zones of the Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits. The semi-official news agency Anatolia has denied this. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Athens According to a report from the Athens News Agency, Prime Minister Metaxas recently stated that the claim that Turkish troops have entered the demilitarized zones of the Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits did not originate from the Turkish capital. The Turkish government has stated that this issue should be handled by the Administrative Council of the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Angora According to reliable sources, the cabinet recently held a meeting and decided to send troops to garrison the Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits. According to rumors, the troops entered the Straits area on the evening of the 16th of this month. However, this has been denied by the semi-official Anatolia News Agency. According to the Treaty of Sèvres after the European War and the Treaty of Lausanne after the Greco-Turkish War, the banks of the Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits are demilitarized zones. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

(Moscow) On the 11th of this month, the Turkish government sent a note to the signatory countries of the Treaty of Lausanne (Britain, France, Italy, Japan, Greece, Yugoslavia, Romania, Bulgaria) and other countries concerned, requesting that Article 18 of the treaty, which deals with the abolition of military preparations in the Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits, be amended. Foreign Minister Litvinov recently submitted a reply to Turkish Ambassador Vasif. It is reported that the content is that the Soviet government has no objection to Turkey's intention, but requests Turkey to provide a guarantee that Soviet fleets will be allowed to pass freely through the two straits. It is generally expected that Turkey will provide a satisfactory response to this request. A senior official recently stated that the relationship between the Soviet Union and Turkey has always been strong, and if the friendship between the two countries can be maintained, the issue of re-fortifying the Straits area will not cause any harm to Russia. People in political circles are not surprised by Turkey's request for two reasons: The Soviet Union did not participate in the Treaty of Lausanne, and the Soviet Union has always maintained that Turkey should enjoy full sovereignty over the Straits area. Once the Dardanelles and Bosporus Straits are re-fortified, they will become the Soviet Union's foremost line of defense, which the Soviet Union welcomes. (Havas dispatch on the 17th)

(London) As soon as the rumor that Turkish troops had violated the Dardanelles Convention and entered the Straits area spread, the Turkish semi-official news agency issued a denial, stating that the claim was absolutely unfounded. The Cabinet Council of Ten Nations held a cabinet meeting this week. The rumor that Turkish troops had entered the Straits area was transmitted from Ankara to Istanbul and then to Paris. Although the French newspapers reported the news, they considered it not entirely credible. According to this rumor, at a cabinet meeting held by Turkey on April 15, presided over by President Kemal, it was decided to occupy the Straits area with military force and station troops there. Last night, Turkish troops had entered this forbidden area. People in London considered this news to be suspicious, because Turkey was requesting to amend the Dardanelles Convention and the countries concerned had agreed to give it sympathetic consideration. Britain sent out a reply today, advising it to raise this issue in a proper form. Therefore, Turkey may not have taken this surprising action so quickly. (Reuters dispatch on the 18th)

Japanese Troops in North China Rotate, Construct Barracks and Airfields in Dongjuzi, Attempting to Make It a Permanent Air and Land Force Base

Tianjin Dispatch Japanese troops in various parts of North China, about 800 of whom belonged to the 1st Division, have reached the end of their tour of duty. On the 13th of this month, they were rotated. The new troops belonged to the Fukuyama Regiment of the 5th Hiroshima Division, about 800 in total. 600 of them arrived at Tanggu on the morning of the 12th on the Japanese military vessel Hongjian Maru and disembarked. They boarded two special trains on the Beijing-Ningbo Railway. About 250 went to Beiping and 250 went to Tangshan and Qian'an County. When the troops going to Beiping passed through Tianjin, Japanese Commander Tada, along with Gendarmerie Commander Ike, Staff Officer Nakai, and Adjutant Kami, went to the station to comfort them and give a speech. The troops going to Tangshan were comforted by Staff Officer Ishii on behalf of Tada. The new Japanese troops in the Third Area of Tianjin and Tangshan all took over their defenses on the same day. The troops rotating in Beiping, Tangshan, and Qian'an County are scheduled to leave China on the 18th, board trains and gather at Tanggu, and take a military vessel to Dalian, and then go to the Northeast to reinforce the defenses. About 200 troops from the 5th Division are expected to arrive in Qinhuangdao on the 17th and disembark there and go to the Changli garrison to be stationed. The total number of Japanese troops stationed in North China is more than 1,800. Only a quarter of them have been rotated. Most of them will be rotated after the troop strength is reinforced in May and June this year. At present, the Tianjin Garrison Headquarters is keeping the reinforced troop strength and the names of the commanders secret. However, it is almost certain that the number of troops will be 8,000, organized into a mixed brigade. Regarding the reason for the troop increase, the Tianjin Japanese Garrison Headquarters will

Regarding the reason for the troop increase, there was a rumor that the commander would be a lieutenant general. It is also a certainty that Tada will remain in his position and be promoted to lieutenant general. Chief of Staff Nagami may also be promoted to major general at the same time. Therefore, there is hope that he will be reappointed. The issue of barracks related to the reinforcement of troops, which the Japanese side was quite worried about before, has recently been resolved. That is, 1,300 mu of land in Liming Village, Dongjuzi, Tianjin, will be occupied to build magnificent barracks. This place was once occupied by the Japanese side as an airfield last year, but the construction was subsequently removed. Now, it has been occupied again. They claim to be giving compensation for the land, but it has not been paid yet. 800 mu of the land belonged to former Governor Li Chun, 500 mu belonged to the Beijing-Ningbo Railway, and more than 40 mu belonged to the people. In addition, there is still nearly 1,000 mu of empty land at the northern end of that section, which the Japanese side is still planning to occupy and build a firewood airfield, combining the area into an air and land base. More than 1,000 workers have been mobilized, about 20 Japanese people are supervising the work, more than 100 large carts are transporting bricks and earth, and more than 10 trucks are transporting materials. The construction is progressing very actively. It is said that the total cost of the project is 400,000 yuan, and the Hongji Company has contracted to build it, with a deadline of five months. In addition to the 500,000 bricks stored in the Japanese barracks at Haiguang Temple, which have been transported to be used, 2.5 million bricks have been purchased from the Tianlong Shengxing brick kilns in Dongjuzi and 2.5 million bricks have been purchased from the Rongxing brick kilns in Xiyingmen. It is easy to imagine how many houses will be built from this alone.

Recently, the Japanese side has also set up an aviation branch in the Japanese concession in Tianjin, and appointed Yamaguchi Masao as the director, specializing in handling aviation liaison between China and foreign countries. Since January, one or two Japanese military planes have flown in daily from foreign countries, carrying mail or passengers, or sometimes carrying Japanese military officers to inspect various places. They all use our China Aviation Corporation airfield in Dongjuzi for their flights. The planes that arrive daily are "127", "128", "129", "132", "130", "140", "502", and "504". Each time they land, people from the Japanese military headquarters go to take care of the passengers and mail. In effect, they have opened up an air route themselves and are using it for regular airmail. (16th)

Shandong Province: The Rising Yellow River Water Levels Cause Concern. The Ice Flood Level is Only Slightly Lower Than the Major Flood Level. There is No Guarantee Whether This Year's Major Flood Will Be Safe.

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River is the Only Major Disaster in North China. Shandong Province is Located in the Lower Reaches. The River Flows Through Areas Starting from Pu Prefecture, Passing Through More Than Twenty Counties, and Entering the Sea at Lijin. There are Numerous Risky Embankments Along the Banks, Which are Very Precarious. Recently, Just as the Breach Was Blocked, News of the Ice Flood Arrived. Judging from the Situation, There is No Guarantee Whether a Breach Can be Avoided During this Year's Major Flood. According to the Yellow River's Annual Flood Period, There are Three Stages: the Ice Flood, the Peach Blossom Flood, and the Major Flood. The Ice Flood and Peach Blossom Flood are Both Very Short in Duration and Easier to Prevent. However, During the Major Flood, the Water Level is High and the Duration is Long. Every Year During the Transition from Summer to Autumn, the Floodwaters from Shaanxi and Gansu Provinces in the Upper Reaches are Like a Released Flood, Rushing Down Thousands of Miles, Making Prevention Difficult and Often Leading to Breaches. In Shandong Province, After the Breach at Gongjiaba in Lijin in the Lower Reaches, Another Breach Occurred at Lisheng Village in the Upper Reaches in 1925, Flooding Various Counties in Western Shandong. In Recent Years, Breaches Have Occurred in the Changyuan Area of Hebei Province Every Year. Last Year, a Breach Occurred Again at Jingzhuang in Dong'a County, Shandong Province, Flooding Western Shandong and Northern Jiangsu, Shaking the Nation. Although the Breach Has Now Been Blocked and the Closure Work Completed, News Has Arrived that the Peach Blossom Flood Season is Approaching. Melting Snow from Areas Such as Suiyuan and Baotou is Rushing Downstream into Shandong, Causing Shandong's River Works to Enter a Serious State Again. On the 14th, the Water Level at Kangtun and Zhukou in the Upper Reaches of Shandong Suddenly Rose by More Than One Meter. The Water Level at Lisheng Village Even Reached 58.5 Inches, Which is Startling. In Previous Years, the Peach Blossom Flood Has Never Seen Such High Water Levels. The Water Level is Only 9.2 Inches Lower Than the Major Flood in 1931. It is Recorded that the Highest Water Level at Lisheng Village in 1931 Was 57.41 Meters, the Highest Water Level in 1932 Was 57.28 Meters, the Highest Water Level in 1933 Was 57.1 Meters, the Highest Water Level in 1934 Was 57.6 Inches, and the Highest Water Level in 1935 Was 56.8 Inches. The Water Levels in 1933 and 1934 Cannot be Relied Upon Because the Breach at Changyuan Had Not Yet Been Blocked. The Difference Between the Water Level in 1931 and This Year's Peach Blossom Flood is More Than 7 Inches. As for the Water Level During the Major Flood, the Highest Water Level in 1931 Was 58.67 Meters, the Highest Water Level in 1932 Was 58.38 Meters. In 1933, the Breach at Changyuan Occurred Again, and the Water Level at Lisheng Village Was Mimicked at 58.5 Inches. The Water Level in 1935 Was 59.15 Inches. By Comparison, the Maximum Water Level During the Current Peach Blossom Flood is Only About One Meter Lower. This Phenomenon is All Due to the Silt Accumulation in the River, the Rising Riverbed, and the Silt Accumulation at the River's Mouth, Which Impedes Discharge. If Plans are Not Made Quickly, When the Major Flood Arrives and the Water Level Rises, There is a Fear that Another Breach May Occur, Making it Difficult to Avoid. (16th)

Furthermore, Zhang Dingcheng Recently Led More Than One Hundred Bandits, Carrying Sharp Browning Pistols and Light Machine Guns, a Total of More Than One Hundred Weapons, Through Chuxi to Xiachikeng Shuikou Dam, Bordering Pinghe, Yongding, and Dabu, to Rob Zhongkeng Village in Jinfeng Village, Yongding, at Around Nine O'Clock at Night. Anhui Tea Business Tax Decides Tax Rate Standards, and the Candidates for the Heads of Each Bureau are Also Determined

Anqing Correspondence: The Anhui Department of Finance, Since this Year's Tea Season has Arrived, in Accordance with Custom, Decided to Set Up Tea Business Tax Bureaus in Ten Places Including Xiuning County, Xiuyi County, Shilimen, Jintai, Xuanlangguang, Tongling, Zhidong, Mabao, Maotanchang, Huoshan, and Qilihe. Currently, the Heads of Each Bureau Have Been Determined. Xu Zhiqin is the Head of Xiuning County Bureau, Liu is the Head of Xiuyi County Bureau, Long is the Head of Shilimen, Wang Aiquan is the Head of Jintai Bureau, Ting is the Head of Xuanlangguang, Ting is the Head of Tongling, Yi Yanchen is the Head of Zhidong, Hu is the Head of Mabao, Chang is the Head of Huoshan, Jia Ang is the Head of Maotanchang, and Kan is the Head of Qilihe. The Tea Tax Quotas are as Follows: Xiuning County 43,000 Yuan, Xiuyi County 35,000 Yuan, Shilimen 18,000 Yuan, Jintai 17,000 Yuan, Xuanlangguang 16,000 Yuan, Tongling 6,500 Yuan, Zhidong 5,500 Yuan, Mabao 35,000 Yuan, Huoshan 25,500 Yuan, Maotanchang 14,500 Yuan, Qilihe 7,500 Yuan.

Regarding the Standards for Tax Rates, they Have also Been Assigned. For Xiuning, Xiuyi, Shilimen, and Zhidong, the Standard Tax Rate for Local Tea is 97.5 Cents per 100 Jin, and the Standard Tax Rate for Foreign Tea is 48 Cents per 100 Jin. For Jing, Xuan, Tong, Ma, Mao, Huo, and Qi, the Standard Tax Rate is 1.2 Yuan per 100 Jin. Tea is Not Divided into Green or Black Tea, and Packaging is Not Distinguished Between Boxes or Loose Packaging. The Weight is Recognized and Calculated Proportionally. The Capital is Taxed at 6 per Thousand for Foreign Tea and 15 per Thousand for Local Tea, Based on the Standard Number Set. The Customary Practice of Deducting the Skin is Applied. Each is Taxed According to the Net Weight. Loose Packaging is Taxed According to the Actual Weight. There Should Be No Items such as Deducting the Skin. As for the Calculation Method for Skin Deduction by Each Bureau, it Should be Listed Before the Tax Collection and Submitted for Approval. Regarding the Calculation Value for Standard Tea, Flower Tea, and Tea Chips, the Calculation Method Set in the Old Case Should be Used. Separate Approval Should be Made, and the List Should be Circulated for Compliance. Regarding the Discount Standards Set in Items 1 and 2, Unless There are Major Special Changes, Which are Re-Established by the Provincial Government, No Matter What the Situation, the Collection Agencies Must Not Freely Expand, Contract, or Change Them. Miscellaneous Writings on Rural Hubei: Our Newspaper Dispatches a Reporter to Yangxin After the Disaster

Our Reporter Visits Yangxin: Having Heard that the Road to Yangxin Was Raided by Bandits, this Reporter Bought a Boat to Wuxue. On the Morning of the 31st, I Took a Steamer Westward from Wuxue. At 4 PM, the Boat Arrived at the Old Site of Yangxin County, Which Has Been Abandoned for a Long Time. Only Ruins Remain. The County is One of the Largest in Southern Hubei, Covering an Area of 3,805.0 Square Kilometers, Extending 200 Li from East to West and 190 Li from North to South. There are Many Mountains and Few Fields in the Entire Territory. Paddy Fields Account for One-Half, Suitable for Rice Cultivation, Which Can Provide Food for Four Months. Dry Land Accounts for Two-Thirds, Producing Sweet Potatoes, Ramie, Wheat, Barley, Yams, Cotton, Sesame, Mung Beans, Broad Beans, Soybeans, Peas, Buckwheat, Sorghum, Corn, etc., Which Can Provide Food for Eight Months. Except for Ramie, Which is Completely Exported, and Cotton, Which is Woven into Coarse Cloth and Sold in Jiangxi, the Rest is Only for Consumption in the County. The Fields are Divided into Three Grades: High-Grade Fields Total 283,199 Mu, Middle-Grade Fields Total 11,437 Mu, and Low-Grade Fields Total 2,825 Mu. The Fushui River Basin is All Fertile Land, and the Areas Within the Three Major Dikes of Gehu, Haikou, and Sigu are Also Mostly Bountiful. Mineral Products Include Coal from Tanshan Bay, Yanxia, and Longgang, Copper from Jilong Mountain, and Niter and Sulfur from Zhoupai Market. Large Lakes Producing Fish Include Fuyuan, Hama, Liangjian, Ditou Dongchun, Zhonghu, and Jiajie. Fish are Extremely Abundant. In Addition, Ten Pieces of Cloth from Each County, Yangshan Leather, and Paper from Yangshan are All Well-Known. Therefore, with a Population of 640,000, People Can Live in Self-Sufficiency. Commerce is Most Prosperous in the County Seat. Longgang and Yanxia are Collection Points for Cotton and Ramie at the Border Area of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. Fuchi is the Mouth of the Yangtze River, as well as Fuyuankou, Sanxikou, Datian, Yangxin, Paishi, Baishapu, Xintanpu, etc., Which are All Famous Market Towns. Since the Destruction During the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, People Have Been Recuperating and Have Not Suffered from War for More Than Eighty Years. In 1929, the Communist Bandits Rampaged for Several Years Without Being Pacified. Following the Severe Drought the Previous Year, There Was a Major Flood Last Year. The Vitality Was Exhausted. It is Estimated that 160,000 People Died, 150,000 Became Refugees, and 40,000 Fled. More Than 20,000 Houses Were Burned Down, and Fertile Fields Were Turned into Lush Grass. Yangxin People Call for Discussion of the Bandit Disaster. It is Said that Education in the County is Developed. In 1924, There Were More Than 600 Middle School Graduates in the County, Known as the New Faction. They Are on Par with the Old Faction Who Serve as Local Gentry, and Fight Each Other Like Fire and Water. As a Result, the New Faction Failed and Sought Revenge, and Joined the Communist Party. It Erupted in 1929. On January 20, 1930, the Red Army Captured the County Seat. All the Old Faction Gentry Were Killed. The Entire County and Dragon Port, Dragon Mountain, Yanxia, ​​Mushi Port, Sanxikou, Paishi, and Datian All Fell into Important Bandit Nests. Those New Faction Bandits, were even more regard citizens as livestock. About 200,000 People Died or Fled. Afterwards, a Large Army Advanced to Suppress Them, and No One Knows How Many Died from Labor or Rotation. The Current Population is Only More Than 400,000, and There Are Only More Than 80,000 Able-Bodied Men. Talking About the Past, It is Heartbreaking.

The Entire County Began to be Recovered Last Year. The Main Force of the Red Bandits Has Been Expelled. Scattered Bandits Have Not Yet Been Eradicated, But They are All in the Mountainous Areas and Dare Not Go to the Plains Again. Local District Offices Have Been Set Up, Divided into Five Districts. The Baojia System Has Also Been Reorganized, Comprising 50 Lianbao, 816 Bao, 7,802 Jia, 88,834 Households, and 462,412 People. There are a Total of 87,014 Able-Bodied Men. More Than 40,000 People Have Been Organized into Civil Defense Teams. The People Have More Than 1,000 Guns. Currently, the First District is the Jia District, the Second District is the Self-Defense District, and the Third, Fourth, and Fifth are the Qingxiang Districts. Many Civilian Houses Were Destroyed, and the Villagers Had Nowhere to Settle. They Built Thatched Huts. The County Government Was Also Burned Down. The Commissioner's Office of the Second District is Located in the Old Inn. Everything is Simple and Crude. The So-Called Villages Have No Ten Households Living Side by Side. One Can See the Extent of the Destruction. However, the Bandit Defense Works, Such as Fortified Villages and Stockades, are Scattered Everywhere. All Eyes Can See are Enclosures. There are Ten Villages, Thirteen Bao, Thirty Blockhouses, and 556碉樓, a Total of 610. All of These are Made from the Blood and Sweat of the People. In All the Counties of Hubei, it Can Be Said That There are the Most. Recently, the Remaining Bandits Have Risen Up Again in the Border Area of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. Chongyang, Tongcheng, and Tongshan Have All Been Harassed. Only Those Who Dare to Enter Yangxin are the Ones Who Achieve Results with Blockhouse Politics.

On April, 1935, the Rain Was Pouring Down, and I Could Not Go to the Countryside. So, I Went to the Commissioner's Office to Visit Li Huiwu, the Commissioner of the Second District and Concurrent County Chief of Yangxin. As It Happened, Li Went to Beijing. Secretary Li Weixin Received Me and Told Me About the Recovery and Rural Plans. What Has Already Been Implemented and is Effective, Relief for Disaster Victims, Has Been Issued More Than Ten Times, Divided into Seven Types: Emergency Relief, Agricultural Relief, Shelter, Price Stabilization, Work Relief, Relief Rice, and Winter Clothing. After the Refugees are Sheltered, They Are Dispersed to Return to Agriculture. The Elderly, Weak, Disabled, and Homeless, as well as Orphans, Are Accommodated in the Disabled Relief Home and the Disaster Child Education Center. Enrolling and Appeasing Those Who Surrender, 8,250 People Have Renewed Themselves. Each Person Receives a Lecture by the Commissioner, is Supervised by the Baojia Chief, and is Given Real Protection. Reorganizing Donations and Taxes, Each Mu of Field is Subject to a Regular Tax of 36 Cents, an Additional County Government Donation of 12 Cents, a School Donation of 6 Cents, a Dike Donation of 26 Cents, and a National Defense Donation of 9 Cents, for a Total of 81.6 Cents. Ramie Donation, Bamboo and Wood, Incense Paper, House Number, Township, Tea Leaf Boat Donation License, Salt Jin Surcharge, Baojia, Petition, Boat Registration, Tourist, Boatman, Various Donations, and Food Party Fees Have All Been Abolished to Alleviate the People's Difficulties. Transportation and Water Conservancy, Roads That Have Been Repaired and Opened to Traffic Include Yangda, Yangrui, Xinyang, Xintong, and Huaxi. Five Lines That Have Been Repaired But Not Completed Include Xin, Yangqi, Longyan, Xi, and Chaxi. Most of the Construction is Done Through Work Relief. In Terms of Water Conservancy, in Addition to Repairing the Gehu, Haikou, and Sigu Two Major Dikes, Each Bao is Limited to Repairing a New Dike. Adjusting Finance, Cooperative Methods are Promoted. The Provincial Disaster Relief Association Appropriated 10,000 to Help Farmers, as well as the Rural Finance Relief Office, the Farmers Bank, and the Chinese Righteous Relief Association, etc., Separately Lending Money to Form Nine Paper Industry Marketing Cooperatives with 340 Members, Lending 9,489.63 Yuan. Twenty-Four Reclamation and Utilization Cooperatives with More Than 480 Members Lending 9,600 Yuan, 459 Rural Cooperative Preparatory Societies, With 16,659 社, Timely Give Them Cattle Seeds Lending 86,90 Yuan, Developing Real Estate, A Group Farm Was Founded Somewhere 15 Miles From the City, and a County Nursery Was Established, and Staff Member Jiang Jie Was Sent to Guide a Visit to the Farm. Because the Muddy After the Rain, We Only Visit the Nursery and the County Middle School. The Nursery is Located at Taohuajing, About Two Miles Outside the West Gate. It is the Head of the Sixteen Springs in That Carp. The Water Clear and Can 鯉 人. The Garden is Planted with Vegetables, Fruits, and Rice and Wheat. The Scale is Not Large, and the Arrangement is Well-Organized. The Suspended Middle School is Located in the City. There Are Only 100 Yuan in Expeditures a Month. The Teachers are Staff Members of the Commissioner's Office and Local People, and Work Entirely on a Voluntary Basis. The Equipment is Simple, and it Goes Without Saying That the Spirit is Commendable. In Addition, There Are Ten Short-Term Primary Schools, Eight People's Schools, Six District Primary Schools, and 58 Lianbao Primary Schools. All Are Suffering from Financial Difficulties and There is a Tendency to Interrupt Their Activities.

Yangxin's Abundance of Barren Fields, May Be the First in the Various Counties of Southern Hubei. It Can Be Pointed Out That There Are More Than 50,000 Mu of Barren Fields Within the Sigu Dike. Speaking of the Entire County, Although There Are No Accurate Statistics, It is Roughly More Than 30 to 40%. Because of the Reduction in Farmers, and the Lack of Plowing Cattle, It is a Pity That Fertile Fields are Barren. Therefore, the Rural Economy is Also Extremely Dry. As for the Mu Donation, It is Relatively Lighter Than Before, But Still Not What the Country Can Do. There are Quite a Few Complaints About the Urgent Call. The Chamber of Commerce Held an Emergency Meeting Yesterday Because the Finance Committee Increased the Commercial Donation to Discuss Coping with It. The Outcome is Unknown. There is Still One Thing Worth Mentioning, Namely, Strict Prohibition of Opium. The People in Southern Hubei Have a Preference for Smoking and Gambling, Especially Opium. Yangxin is No Exception. However, Yangxin Has Made Considerable Achievements in Opium Prohibition. Initially, the Communist Party Killed All Those Who Smoked Opium. The Smokers Then Gathered in the County Seat. There are Two Shops with Fortune Remembered as The Brand, and Forty-One Opium Dens. Even Though They Survived the Disaster, They Continue to Emit Mist and Swallow Clouds, Just Like Before. The Red Bandits Were Suppressed, and Opium Poison Spread Throughout the Countryside Again. The Commissioner's Office Issued a Strict Prohibition Order. All Ten Shops and Opium Dens Were Closed Down. Opium Offenders Were First Sent to the Abstinence and Marriage Hospital for Compulsory Abstinence. Those Who Repeated the Offense Were Punished with 200 Lashes According to Military Law. Those Who Supplied Others with Opium Were Punished with 400 Lashes. No Fines Were Imposed, and No Licenses Were Sold. It is Heard That 324 People Have Already Quit, and 552 People are Currently Quitting. Although Those Who Secretly Smoke or Supply Others with Opium Have Not Yet Been Eradicated, They No Longer Dare to Do So Openly.

Songjiang: Two More Robbers are Captured in the Rice Store Robbery Case

Shen Zhenqing, a Farmer in Zhujia Village, Pudong, Was Robbed on the Night of the Fifth. He Immediately Gathered Neighbors to Arrest the Robbers. One of the Robbers, Shen Rongyi, Was Wounded in the Struggle. He Was Sent to Songjiang the Day Before Yesterday, But Died Midway. Yesterday, the Prosecutor's Office Dispatched Personnel to Investigate. It is Learned that in this Case, the First Sub-Bureau Captured Two More Robbers, Bing Shengsao from Caoqi Village, and Xu Jinfa from Ruqi Village. They Were Sent to Songjiang Today.

Suzhou: President of the Judicial Yuan Arrives in Suzhou for Inspection

Ju Zheng, President of the Judicial Yuan, In Order to Investigate the Judiciary in Various Provinces, He Recently Went to Shanghai from Hangzhou to Inspect the Judicial Organs in Shanghai. On the Evening of the 17th, He Took a Train from Shanghai to Suzhou. He Arrived at Suzhou Station at 1 AM on the 18th. Zhu Shusheng, President of the Jiangsu High Court, Lu Meiyi, President of the District Court, Deng Xianghai, County Chief, and Prison Wardens Were All at the Station to Greet Him. After President Ju Got Off the Train, He Shook Hands with All the Welcoming Personnel and Went Into the City by Car. He Stayed at No. 4 Xinfu Lane, Shiquan Street. He Was Accompanied by His Wife and Five or Six Other People. At Around 9 AM Yesterday (18th), President Ju First Went to the Jiangsu High Court on Daoyin Street for Inspection. He Was Accompanied by Zhu, President of the High Court, and Sun, Chief Prosecutor, to Visit Various Departments and Civil and Criminal Courts, and Inquired with Concern. He Then Went to the Wu County District Court, Jiangsu Re-Examination Institute, Jiangsu Third Prison, High Court Detention Center, and Other Judicial Organs and Prisons for Inspection. At Noon, County Chief Deng and Others Held a Banquet to Entertain President Ju. It is Heard that President Ju Needs to Take a Train Back to Nanjing in the Evening.

Voices on the Earth-Moving Monopoly Case

The County Government Received an Order from the Province that Wu County's Shitae, Ronghua, and Lao Zhixing Earth-Moving Companies had Arbitrarily Increased the Price of Earth and Committed Illegal Monopoly, Ordering the Recovery of More Than 100,000 Gold Coins in Illegal Profits as Opium Suppression Funds. The County Government Immediately Summoned and Arrested the Directors of Each Earth-Moving Company, Sun Jinbiao, and Three Others, to Recover the Illegal Profits. After This Incident Occurred, the Wu County Opium Suppression Committee Members Zhang Yipeng, Liu Yun, and Sun Danchen All Adopted a Passive Attitude and Resigned from Their Posts. Although County Chief Deng Repeatedly and Sincerely Tried to Persuade Them to Stay, the Officials Have Not Yet Indicated That They Will Abandon Their Resignations. The Day Before Yesterday, People Claiming to be Representatives of Wu County Opium Smokers, Such as Yi Zhenhua, Printed a Large Number of Declarations and Distributed Them to Various Organs and Organizations, Stating That Sun Jinbiao Was a Well-Known Earth Peddler Who Committed All Kinds of Illegal Price Increases and Exploited Opium Smokers. Under the Pressure of Power, the Opium Smokers Had No Grievances to Air. Some People Even Defended Sun Jinbiao and Asked All Sectors to Uphold Justice. After Sun Jinbiao and Others Were Arrested, Because the Previous Increase in Earth Prices Had Not Been Approved by the Provincial Opium Suppression Committee, But Had Been Approved by the County Opium Suppression Meeting, it Could Be Said That They Were Complying with Public Orders. This Time They Were Arrested, They Felt That They Were Not Satisfied, So They Came Up with Reasons and Submitted a Petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Jiangsu Provincial Opium Suppression Committee, Requesting Justice and Ordering the County to Release Them. Yesterday, They Received Instructions from the Provincial Opium Suppression Committee, Which Approved of Their Petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and Ordered Them to Await Instructions from the Provincial Government.

A Notorious Thief is Arrested

Fang, a Notorious Thief Known as "Flying Grass," Had Thirty-Two Followers, All Skilled in Scaling Walls. They Had Been Stealing for Twenty Years. They Came to Beijing Recently from Zhejiang Lake. One of the 32 People, Zeng Guohua, Came to Suzhou from Beijing. At Eighteen, He Stole Two Boxes from Someone's Residence Near Guanzhong Street. He Was About to Fly Off the Roof When He Was Spotted by a Beat Officer. The Beat Officer Approached to Arrest Him. Zeng Leapt Off a Wooden Pole. The Beat Officer Immediately Drew His Gun. Finally, The Thief Jumped Down and Was Arrested. According to His Confession, the Other Thirty-One Accomplices Were Living in Nanjing. All of Them Were Wearing Western Suits and Leather Shoes, Inviting to Travel in the City. Government Officials Would Have Difficulty Recognizing Them. Zeng is Currently Being Detained in the Public Security Bureau Awaiting Interrogation.

Because There Were No Family Members, They Were Placed in a Coffin by Shanbei Three-Picture 　 正 　 and were Responsible for Guarding Them. All of the Deceased's Belongings Were Taken to the Court for Filing. When the Store Discovered It, It Was Immediately Sent to Tongren Hospital for Treatment. At the Time, He Had Drunk Too Much After Taking the Poison, So His Life Was Quite Dangerous.

Changshu: Violent Mobs Open Dams and Destroy River Works

The Second Main River, Which Runs Through the Fourth and Seventh Districts of the County, is Very Important to the Water Conservancy of the Entire County. Last Winter, the County Government Decided to Dredge the Upper and Lower Silt at the Same Time This Spring. The Dam Work Began in Early This Month. However, This Project, Although Beneficial to the Public, is Not Beneficial to the Sand Fields. Therefore, Tan Jiujin Opposed it and Posted Slogans and Gathered for Lectures. The County Government Ordered Tan Pu瓖 to Dredge the River Project. Seven Bailiffs were Sent to the Village to Arrest Tan. Midway, The Were Robbed, and the Bailiffs Were Beaten and Bound. The Hospital of the River Dredging Director (Township Chief) Geng Shimin Was Destroyed. The County Government Has Sent a Large Number of Security Teams to the Village to Suppress Them. The Villagers Are Still United and Unwilling to Disperse. On the Evening of the 17th, They Beat Gongs to Gather People, Excavated the Constructed Dam Foundations at Both Ends of the Main River, Causing River Water to Pour In, and Destroying the Entire River Dredging Project. The Wounded Bailiffs Have Returned to the City to be Treated at the Hospital.

Bengbu: The People's Factory Runs Out of Funds and Shuts Down

The Bengbu People's Factory Was Founded in September 1933 by Personnel Dispatched by the Ministry of Industry. Initially, the Rent from the Gao Family's Property in Houde Lane Was Used as an Annual Expense. At That Time, the House Was Mortgaged to the Bank for 5,000 Yuan as Start-Up Capital. It Was Officially Established on October 20 of That Year. Initially, Two Departments Were Set Up: Dyeing and Weaving. The Products Were Well Received by All Sectors. However, Due to Financial Difficulties, It Faced Repeated Difficulties. Although Director Deng Tried His Best to Support It, He Was Unable to Support It Due to Insufficient Income. The Final Fund Was Exhausted, and It Fell into a State of Stagnation. Moreover, the Factory Building Was Damaged and Unable to be Repaired, and It Collapsed One After Another. The Factory Could Not Maintain its Current State. Recently, It Reported to the Ministry of Industry, Asking the Anhui Provincial Government to Transfer and Receive It. It is Learned That the Provincial Government Has Ordered the Bengbu Public Security Bureau to First Find Out the Assets of the Factory and Report Them in Detail for Reorganization. After Receiving the Order, the Public Security Bureau Has Sent Personnel to Investigate.
