Breaking the Case of the Kidnapping of Zhou Jiasheng: Twelve Male and Female Kidnappers Apprehended for Interrogation; Heavy Rainfalls as a Relentless Judge Interrogates, Then Postpones for Further Investigation; Police Apprehended Another Accomplice Yesterday Morning

Zhou Chunbo, a native of Hubei, ran a cotton yarn business under the name "Tianshengfu" on Guangdong Road, Dehe Lane. His family resided at No. 135 Buban Road, Bobert Lane in the French Concession. He had a three-year-old son named Jiasheng. On the afternoon of the fourth of this month at one o'clock, while being taken out to play by his nanny, Ms. Jin Zhou, a native of Shaoxing, they were suddenly abducted by a group of kidnappers who seized both her and the child. Zhou reported this to the French police, requesting an investigation. Subsequently, the kidnappers repeatedly sent letters to Zhou, demanding a ransom of 50,000 yuan. They initially planned to meet at the Huizhong Hotel, where detectives were waiting in ambush, but the kidnappers failed to appear, resulting in no outcome. Recently, Yu A'gen, the Chinese Chief Detective of the Old Zha Police Station in the Public Concession, apprehended three Shaoxing gang bandits – Bian Guangxian, Mao Tingfa, and Zhang Yongkang – at the intersection of Xizang Road and Nanjing Road and at No. 310 Yunnan Road. It was discovered that they had committed numerous thefts within the concession, and they were handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Now, according to Bian's confession, there were several accomplices, who were scheduled to meet this Friday (i.e., the day before yesterday) at the Sanxingyuan Tea House, No. 5, Lane 932, Tangshan Road. Chief Detective Yu then led Chinese Detectives Lu Gengsheng, Detective Pang Ruiqing, Wang Shusen, Special Agent Zhu Shangwu, and others, along with Bian, to Sanxingyuan to wait in ambush. Subsequently, Chen Jianzhao, Xu Rengui, and Zhu Mingzhi from Shaoxing arrived one after another, and Bian identified them all as accomplices. The detectives then arrested them all and brought them back to the police station. Under questioning, Xu Rengui confessed that Zhou Jiasheng had been kidnapped by them and was currently being held at No. 12 Peideli, Zhangjiazhai Road, Pudong, and that firearms were also located there. Chief Detective Yu immediately led the original team of Chinese detectives, along with Western Detectives Smith and McKay, and French Concession Detective Zhang Ziying, to Pudong at 5:30 p.m. the day before yesterday, amidst torrential rain, to carry out the arrest in coordination with the Pudong Public Security Bureau detectives. First, the detectives ordered Xu Rengui to go forward and knock on the door. Zhang Xibiao, one of the kidnappers, opened the door, but as soon as he opened it halfway, Zhang saw a large number of Chinese and Western detectives behind Xu and, realizing the situation was unfavorable, tried to slam the door shut. However, because there were so many detectives, he could not resist, and the door was pushed open. Zhang then fled out the back door with his accomplices, Jin Fengxiang and Wang Baopin. The detectives guarding the back door immediately gave chase, but due to the rain and slippery conditions, they were unable to catch them. Western Detective McKay immediately fired a shot from his gun, but it missed. The three criminals were finally apprehended after being chased for about eighty yards. The other detectives rushed in through the front door and arrested Ma Liangfu, Ms. Wang Xie, Wang Xiangzhen, and Wang Xiangzhao, and rescued the hostage Zhou Jiasheng from upstairs. At the same time, Jin Zhou (i.e., Zhou's nanny), who was guarding the hostage, was arrested. A brand-new Mauser pistol with seven bullets was found under the pillow, and ten bullets were found in a box. With the permission of the Public Security Bureau, the captured criminals, hostage, and firearms were all taken back to the Old Zha Police Station. Subsequently, according to Bian's confession, another accomplice was hiding at No. 429 Buban Road, and detectives rushed there at around 2:00 a.m. and apprehended Ma Jinda, a native of Shaoxing. Yesterday morning, the police sent the twelve arrested individuals – Chen Jianzhao, Xu Rengui, Zhu Mingzhi, Zhang Xibiao, Jin Fengxiang, Wang Baopin, Ma Liangfu, Ma Jinda, Jin Zhou, Wang Xie, Wang Xiangzhen, and Wang Xiangzhao – to the First Special District Court, Criminal Division One. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang explained the situation and requested detention in accordance with Articles 76 and 101 of the Criminal Procedure Law, stating that the suspects had committed numerous crimes and urgently needed investigation. Judge Feng Shide reviewed the report, briefly questioned Xu Rengui and the others, and ordered their detention, postponing the hearing to a later date. Zhang Xibiao, one of the arrested criminals, had previously been arrested and sent to court by the police in connection with a theft case, but Zhang was cunning and the crime could not be definitively proven, so he was released. However, Zhang did not repent and continued his evil deeds. Now he has been arrested again, and it is unlikely that he will escape the law this time. The French police also apprehended another accomplice in this case yesterday morning.

Shooting of Ms. Hu Wu in Pudong; Four Robbers Arrested; Xu Jinlong…Hu Changfa; Yang Changfu…Pang Hongbin

Regarding the robbery and theft that occurred at the small grocery store opened by Hu Desheng, a native of Qingjiang, at No. 71 Yongchangtian Road, Pudong, on the evening of August 8th of last year at around 8:00 p.m., Hu's wife, Ms. Wu, was shot and killed by the robbers when she went out the back door, entered the neighbor's house, and then went out the front door to call for help. The criminals fled in all directions without a trace. Recently, the Criminal Investigation Brigade of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau learned that the notorious robber Xu Jinlong (also known as Xu Jinbiao, 31 years old, native of Siyang) was hiding at No. 119 Taoyuanzhai, Pudong. Because the case had been delayed for so long, he dared to openly come and go. Therefore, at 7:00 p.m. the night before last, Detective Wu Xiufeng was secretly dispatched across the Huangpu River, together with patrol officer Zheng Xiheng of the Pudong Sub-bureau, to make the arrest. The criminal was arrested near Sanwanchang. Under interrogation, he revealed the whereabouts of his accomplices. At 9:00 a.m. yesterday, Detective Liu Depu was ordered to take the criminal, along with policeman Lu Yinglin of the Pudong Sub-bureau, to No. 2 Yangjiazhai Branch Road to arrest Hu Changfa (37 years old, native of Huai'an, currently running a tea house for a living). They also went to No. 32, Lane 60, behind Tudi Temple to arrest Yang Changfu (54 years old, native of Guanyun, currently a manual laborer at an iron factory), and to a grass shed at No. 6 Hehuagou to arrest Pang Hongbin (32 years old, native of Huai'an, currently a manual laborer at an iron factory). The three criminals were taken back to the Sub-bureau. After a brief interrogation by Chief Zhang of the Sub-bureau, they were handed over to the detectives to be taken back to the Brigade for further investigation.

Wang Tongfu, Head of the Pudong-Songjiang District Defense Corps, Commits Suicide; Family Unable to Save Him Due to Intolerable Malignant Sores

Wang Tongfu, 39 years old, a native of Shanghai, was the head of the Pudong-Songjiang District Defense Corps in western Shanghai. He had been suffering from malignant sores for some time, which were not healing despite repeated medical treatment. The pain became unbearable, and the sores were spreading uncontrollably. Therefore, he suddenly conceived the idea that death was better than life. At 9:00 a.m. yesterday, in his room at No. 177, he committed suicide with a rifle pointed directly at his heart, dying with a hole in his chest. By the time his family found him and tried to help, he had already breathed his last. They reported the incident to the police station, which ordered the local constable Shen Zhaogang to report it to the local court for inspection.

Clues to the Assassination of Lu Rukang in Zhabei; The Bullet Found on Zhang Xiaogen Matches the Bullet Shell from Lu's Assassination

Lu Rukang, a silk merchant residing at No. 9 Renxing Lane, Qingyun Road, Zhabei, was suddenly shot and killed by a group of thugs at around 6:30 a.m. on January 14th. Afterward, the police found a bullet shell at the scene and submitted it to the bureau for record. It is now learned that the Xinzha Police Station of the Public Concession arrested Zhang Xiaogen, a native of Changshu, 34 years old, who was illegally carrying firearms, at Xingle Lane, Avenue Edward VII, at 8:30 p.m. on the 16th. A six-round revolver with serial number 4553 and twenty bullets were found on him, and he was handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Zhang confessed that the gun came from Wu Yongsheng, a clerk at the Lidechang Tinware Shop on Nanwang Street, Nanxiang. However, it has been determined that Zhang's bullets match the bullet shell from the Lu Rukang assassination case. The police bureau is conducting a detailed investigation and research based on this clue.

Shanghai Waterworks Company to Provide Free Drinking Water Beginning May 15th

Every year, at the beginning of summer, the Shanghai Waterworks Company allows residents to draw water from public taps on the roads in areas where there are no water pipe connections. This is done at the request of the Public Works Department to encourage cleanliness and prevent cholera. The Public Works Department recently sent another letter to the company, expressing its gratitude for the previous year's arrangements and requesting that the company continue to do so this year. It is reported that the company has replied, agreeing to continue providing free water as before, starting on May 15th, for the benefit of the common people.

A Weak Daughter-in-Law Dies After Childbirth Under the Tyranny of a Ferocious Mother-in-Law; The Death Is Not Reported to the Daughter's Family; Claimed Death from Illness, But with Injuries on Her Limbs

Wang Miaosheng, a farmer from Wangjiadu, Third Bao, Linjiang Township, Sanlintang Town, Pudong, had a daughter, Wang Cuixin, 24 years old. In May of last year, she married Xu Xiaodi, the son of Xu Xichun, who ran the Xushunxing Coffin Shop in Sanlintang Town. However, because her dowry was meager, she was disliked by her parents-in-law. In particular, her aunt-in-law, Xu Jin (57 years old), was known as a ferocious woman and treated this poor daughter-in-law with extreme disdain and inhuman treatment, which was observed by the neighbors. The young couple was harmonious, but they lacked the ability to be independent and harbored resentment that was difficult to express. Therefore, although Xu Wang Cuixin lived under despotic and tyrannical oppression every day, she was already pregnant. Last month, she gave birth, but her aunt-in-law did not take care of her and instead constantly physically abused her, causing the new mother to suffer severe injuries. She lingered on, eventually becoming ill and in critical condition. Yet, they did not seek medical attention, so she died unjustly the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, her parents-in-law secretly did not notify her family and hastily prepared the body for burial. Wang Miaosheng learned of this and immediately went to stop them, and reported the incident to the Second Sub-bureau of the County Public Security Bureau. Chief Hua of the Bureau ordered the police to arrest and detain Xu Jin. He also ordered the local constable to report the incident to the local court, which appointed Prosecutor Zhang and Coroner Shen to inspect the body at the scene. Xu Wang died of illness, but with injuries on her limbs. They filled out a death certificate, ordered the body to be prepared for burial, and ordered that the case be investigated in accordance with the law.

The Public Works Department Agrees to Convene a Meeting of Rickshaw Merchants; Rickshaw Pullers Petitioned the Taxpayers' Association Yesterday

The Public Works Department sent a letter to rickshaw merchants yesterday, agreeing to convene a meeting to resolve the rickshaw dispute. Rickshaw pullers petitioned the Taxpayers' Association yesterday regarding registration issues. The details are as follows:

Letter from the Public Works Department: The rickshaw merchants of the Special District, in order to resolve all outstanding issues as soon as possible, requested the Public Works Department through their lawyer, Mr. Masters, to convene an equal meeting as soon as possible to discuss a solution. The Public Works Department has agreed and replied yesterday: Sir, I have received your letter of the 15th and understand that your clients wish to hold a meeting with representatives of this bureau as soon as possible to resolve all issues. This bureau agrees. The proposed meeting date is within the next week, on a day that is convenient for your clients. The meeting time is 9:45 a.m., which is most appropriate. Sincerely, Philip, Deputy Director-General of the Public Works Department.

Petition from Rickshaw Pullers: Over fifty rickshaw puller representatives from the Special District, including Chen Guoliang, petitioned the Public Concession Taxpayers' Association at 5:00 p.m. yesterday. They were received by the chairman of the Association, Wang Xiaolai. Chen Guoliang and others first expressed their intentions, stating that they represented over 20,000 unemployed rickshaw pullers, requesting the Rickshaw Committee of the Public Works Department to carry out universal registration, and allow free registration in accordance with the regulations of the French Concession to prevent rickshaw pullers from becoming unemployed. They strongly advocated for the recovery of the Mutual Aid Society and the abolition of the Rickshaw Committee. Mr. Wang accepted the petition and handed it over to the Executive Committee for processing, and encouraged the rickshaw pullers to consider social stability and wait patiently for a solution. The rickshaw pullers were satisfied and returned.

Vegetable Market Fish Vendors Throughout the City Plead for the Fish Market to Open Soon; Recounting the Suffering of Exploitation by Various Trades; Deeply Hoping that the Fish Market Will Be Opened Soon to Relieve Them

The Shanghai Fish Market, a joint venture between government and merchants, which has been prepared by Chairman Du Yuesheng, Standing Directors Fang Jiaobo and Tang Chengzong, and Deputy Managers Wang Xiaoxiang, Zhu Kaiguan, and Sun Guchen, held its inaugural meeting on the 10th of this month and took over on the 17th. All equipment and arrangements are now in place, and the preparatory staff have also begun working, deciding to open for business within the next month, to satisfy the longings of the fish merchants. Yesterday afternoon, representatives of the stallholders in various vegetable markets throughout the city, including Wang Yuanzhou and Xu Danyun, petitioned the board of directors and presented it to Chairman Du Yuesheng, recounting the suffering of various fish trades and requesting the market to open as soon as possible. The board of directors accepted them and promised to adopt their suggestions. The petition is recorded as follows: The case is submitted to the above for review and approval. Representatives Chen Xiufang and others from various vegetable market representatives under the Vegetable Market Stallholders' United Benefit Association reported that recently, fish vendor members of various vegetable markets, seeing that the fish market site had been established for a long time, but fish vendors still had to go to the Sixteen Shops Fish Trade to purchase fish and could not purchase directly from the fish market, the fish trades in the Sixteen Shops, always regarded fish vendors as weak and easy to bully, and indulged in all kinds of means of oppression and tyranny, not to mention. For example, when a fish vendor purchases fish from a fish trade, once contact is made, they cannot but buy it, and when buying a bucket of fish, rotten fish are often mixed into it, regardless of whether the fish vendor can sell it. If they ask to exchange it, they are either shouted at loudly or beaten with old fists. Often, because the fish vendor insists on exchanging it or simply does not buy it, they are beaten by the trade members, and there is no one to whom they can complain. Also, the fish trades often mix ice cubes into the fish to increase the weight of the ice and obtain illegal and unexpected profits. For example, when buying twenty catties of fish, five catties of ice cubes are mixed in. If the ice is removed, there are only fifteen catties of fish, but the bill is still calculated as twenty catties of pure fish. Moreover, there is no standard for how much ice is mixed in, unless you know the trade members, you cannot avoid this kind of fish and ice mixed selling exploitation. As for trade transactions, when paying, if the fish trade owes the fish vendor two jiao of silver coins, they will only give two jiao of small silver coins. Some even delay payment by claiming that the accountant is busy and will not find it immediately, deliberately delaying the time, and the fish vendor, because they are in a hurry to get to the vegetable market and fear the trade's power, dare not argue, swallowing their anger and leaving. What is hateful is that they often take in the fish vendor's real money and immediately take out counterfeit money and exchange it with the fish vendor. The fish trades use all kinds of cunning means. How do they know that the fish vendors are operating on a small capital, and their parents, wives, and children depend on this for a living. After such an unexpected loss, a family of several people is in immediate danger. All of these are the great sufferings of fish vendors. In short, the fish trade sees fish vendors as enemies and is exhaustive in cheating and exploiting fish vendors. Now that the Shanghai Fish Market has been established, it is appropriate to give up the fish trades and purchase and sell directly to the market, to avoid all kinds of bullying by the fish trades. All fish stallholders unanimously requested Xiufang and others to report to your office and request the fish market to allow direct purchases. Xiufang and others dare not lag behind in the cause of promoting benefits and eliminating harms. Since they have been requested by various stallholders, they should report to your office. Based on this, the fish trade and the fish vendors have a close relationship in daily transactions and should be cared for. However, they are subject to various oppressions. Today, the market is declining, and the poor stallholders make a living by selling, and the impact is difficult to profit from. How can they be subjected to such oppression and exploitation by the fish trades? Yuanzhou and others are members of the fish vendors and are well aware of the suffering of the fish vendors. If we continue to delay, the fish vendors in various vegetable markets will be doomed. Considering the purpose of the government in establishing your market, it was originally to promote the fishing industry, develop fishing profits, and relieve the suffering of fishermen. And the fish vendors have a great relationship with the fishing industry. Since representatives Chen Xiufang and others from various vegetable markets have reported one after another, Yuanzhou and others dare not sit idly by. Therefore, a meeting of representatives from various vegetable markets was convened on the 14th of this month. The result was that the above-mentioned suffering of the fish vendors needs to be relieved. Therefore, it is appropriate to submit a document requesting your market to sympathize with the weak and suffering fish vendors and allow them to purchase fish directly from your market, so as not to be deceived by the Sixteen Shops Fish Trade. This will be a great benefit. Respectfully submitted, Du, Chairman of the Shanghai Fish Market, Wang Yuanzhou, representative of the Joint Office of the United Benefit Association of Vegetable Market Stallholders in Various Districts of Shanghai, Xu Danyun of Huainan, Ren Haizhou of Zhabei, Xia Kaicheng of Yinxiang, Qiu Zhensheng of the First Special District, Pan Lianfang of the Second Special District.

Memorial Service for Li Yanshi Today at the Lake Society in the Afternoon

Mr. Li Yanshi of Wuxing studied law and political science in Germany and Austria at an early age. After returning to China, he served as a professor in the Ministry of Justice and at Peking University and Chaoyang Zhengzhi School. Later, in view of the fact that China's electrical industry was still in its infancy and needed promotion to help industry and commerce and benefit rural areas, he successively operated the Changzhou Qishu Power Plant, the Wuxing Electric Company, and the Wuhu Mingyuan Electric Company, with remarkable achievements. At the same time, he organized the Zhejiang Provincial Private Electric Industry Federation and the National Private Electric Industry Federation to communicate and regulate the industry. The private electric industry has been protected, and the industry has benefited greatly. As for local public welfare and social undertakings, he did his best to support them. He worked hard and fell ill, and died of illness at his Shanghai residence at 7:00 p.m. on March 9th of this year. Various groups will hold a memorial service at the Lake Society at 2:00 p.m. today (the 19th). Anyone who has friendship with Mr. Li can participate.

The Trial of Mr. Graff, General Manager of American Oriental Bank: Defense Lawyer Beauregard Evades Questions, Case Too Complex, Hearing Adjourned, Graff Remains on Bail

The case of Mr. Graff, a German national and the General Manager of the now-defunct American Oriental Bank, accused of fraud and embezzlement, has undergone its initial trial at the First Special District Court. He was sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined one thousand yuan. Graff, unsatisfied with the verdict, retained lawyers Chen Tingrui, Fei Sigaolu, and Man to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The Shanghai Municipal Council (工部局), which initially filed the public prosecution against Graff through their lawyer Beauregard (博良), and Ru Baoyi (汝葆彝) felt that the initial sentence was not enough to atone for Graff's crimes. Therefore, they also filed an appeal. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhong Qing of the Second Branch of the High Court opened an investigative hearing. Graff was summoned, and Chiang Bao-liang (蔣葆良) was appointed as the translator. The three lawyers representing Graff, Chen, Fei, and Gao, immediately requested that the court order Beauregard, the Shanghai Municipal Council lawyer, to recuse himself from the case. After a debate with lawyer Ru Baoyi, the court deemed that there was no need for Beauregard to recuse himself and rejected the application. However, the three lawyers, Chen, Fei, and Gao, argued that their request could not be rejected solely by the investigating judge. They repeatedly pleaded and requested that the case be adjourned to allow them the opportunity to study and explore the reasons for the Shanghai Municipal Council's appeal. Judge Zhong, considering the complexity of the case, agreed to postpone the hearing. Graff was allowed to remain out on his original bail.

Haining Road: Sand-Casting Workshop Boiler Explosion, Apprentice Shi Dalong Scalded

At the sand-casting workshop opened by Cao Yumen at No. 5, Lane 76, Haining Road in the British Concession, an accident occurred around 9 AM the day before yesterday. While workers were on the job, a boiler's pressure unexpectedly rose too high, causing it to explode with a loud bang. The sound shook the neighborhood, and houses rattled. Apprentice Shi Dalong, 18 years old and from Jiangbei, was scalded by boiling water on the spot. He was immediately taken to the Chinese Red Cross Hospital for treatment by patrol car. Doctors said his injuries were quite severe. Cao Yumen, the owner of the workshop, was taken to the Huizi (匯司) police station for questioning.

Medical Circle

Dr. Song Guowei is Good at Treating Hemorrhoids: Dr. Song Guowei, a native of Jiading, Jiangsu Province, went to Germany in 1927 to study medicine at the affiliated hospital of the University of Göttingen. He had years of clinical practice. Seeing the prevalence of hemorrhoids in China, he devoted himself to research and achieved great success. He returned to China six years ago and set up a clinic. He has cured no fewer than 2,580 patients. The "Que Zhi Bing" (却痔病, Hemorrhoid Remedy) injection, patented and sold exclusively by the Shanghai Xinya Pharmaceutical Factory, is widely used by major hospitals and famous doctors throughout the country. Recently, his father invented a new "Po Zhi Er" (破痔兒, Hemorrhoid Breaker) suppository, which is also popular in various ports and has the same effect as "Que Zhi Bing." Dr. Song's clinic is now located at No. 214, Jing'an Building, Tongfu Road intersection, Jing'an Temple Road. The number of patients visiting daily is quite large.

Tong Hanchun Does Not Have Branch Stores: Tong Hanchun Pharmacy (童涵春藥號) on Xiaodongmen Street was founded during the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty. It has a history of more than 100 years. It is trusted by all sectors and is considered to be a genuine old pharmacy. All stores are head offices and there are no branch stores in the local and foreign ports. The Tong Yanchun Pharmacy (童延春) North City branch store newly opened on North Nicheng Bridge (北泥城橋) reported in yesterday's newspaper is another company that has nothing to do with the Tong Hanchun (童涵春) with over 100 years of history.

Cai's Smoking Cessation Center Celebrates One Week Anniversary: Mr. Cai Xuchen, a traditional Chinese medicine doctor, has extensive knowledge and experience. Seeing the harm of opium spreading throughout the country and lacking good medicine to save people, he founded a smoking cessation center at No. 4, Weishui Lane, Ningbo Road last year on the first day of the 8th month. He carefully prepares secret Chinese medicine formulas for smoking cessation, assessing each patient's physical condition, differentiating between deficiency and excess, and heat and cold, and prescribing medicine accordingly. The formula allows patients to not feel pain and not have to lose time from work. The long term goal is for the addiction to be completely eliminated within a month. Since the center opened last year, the number of people seeking treatment has been endless. More than 100 people have quit smoking. To celebrate the one-week anniversary and to give preferential treatment to those who wish to quit smoking, he will provide free consultations and medicine for two months. A registration fee of only two jiao will be collected. At this time when the government is strictly prohibiting smoking, all smoking compatriots should quickly go to quit.

Sheng Ling Chun is Selling Well During Spring: It is easy for chronic diseases to occur during the Spring season. The most common disease among men is kidney deficiency and spermatorrhea. French Sheng Ling Chun (攝生靈) is an effective medicine specifically for this disease. It has been sold in China for over ten years, exclusively managed by the Yuan Dong Longhua Li Hang at No. 457 Hankou Road in Shanghai. Due to the climate, sales are particularly strong, with pharmacies from various local and foreign ports purchasing every day, and they are overwhelmed. It is also reported that those who have taken the medicine say that the effects are indeed unique. After taking the medicine, you can sleep peacefully and there is no need to worry about losing valuable essence during sleep. The more you take the medicine, the stronger you get. There are no stimulants mixed in. Each bottle is a 10-day supply and only costs 1 yuan and 5 jiao. The Wing On Company and other pharmacies sell this product.

Education News

The 12th Annual Meeting of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture: Approved the Operating Budget for Fiscal Year 25, Determined the Amount of Subsidies for Cultural Institutions, Announced the Candidates for Scientific Grants, Mr. Cai Yuanpei Re-elected as Chairman

The Board of Directors of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture held its 16th annual meeting at the Cangzhou Hotel in Shanghai yesterday morning, starting at 9:00 AM. The meeting included reports on various matters, discussion of various operating budgets, determination of funding for educational and cultural institutions, and re-election of officers and allocation of responsibilities. The list of candidates for scientific research grants for fiscal year 25 was also announced. Our Shanghai reporter has the following details:

University Entrance Exam Questions Must Follow High School Curriculum Standards

(Nanjing, 18th) The Ministry of Education received a report from the Peiping Municipal Education Association stating that when the Ministry of Education announced the secondary school curriculum standards in 1933, it issued an order stating that all universities should set entrance examination questions according to the secondary school curriculum standards to ensure continuity. However, according to reports in Peiping newspapers, some universities in Peiping are including Party Doctrine as a subject in this year's summer enrollment. The Ministry of Education's previously issued secondary school curriculum standards include Civics but not Party Doctrine. This not only makes it difficult for secondary school graduates to apply, but it also contradicts the Ministry's orders. The members of the association, realizing this, proposed that all universities in the country be ordered to set entrance examination questions in accordance with the previously issued secondary school curriculum standards during this year's summer enrollment so that secondary school graduates have a curriculum to base their applications on. The Ministry of Education is investigating the issue. Students applying to specialized schools or above this summer have completed their high school courses in accordance with the senior high school curriculum standards promulgated in November 1932. The relevant schools should base their entrance examinations this summer on the aforementioned curriculum standards to ensure continuity. It is hereby ordered that all high schools under your jurisdiction be instructed to comply.

Hebei Province Decides to Hold Joint Examinations

(Beiping, 18th) It was previously rumored that the current middle school joint examinations in Peiping would be cancelled. Now, the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee has decided that the joint examination system is a central government regulation, and the results of this examination will be used for performance evaluations. Therefore, it has been decided to hold the examinations as usual.

Tianjin Expands People's Education Center

(Tianjin, 18th) The Tianjin Municipal Government has allocated 20,000 yuan to expand the People's Education Center to promote public education.

Jiangsu Education Inspection Team Arrives in Yongning

(Yongning, 18th) The Jiangsu Education Inspection Team, consisting of Wu Zeng, Jie Jinyingyuan, and Pan Ren, arrived in Yongning from Guangdong for inspection.

Jiang Kanghu to Lecture Today

Dr. Jiang Kanghu has been lecturing at the New Sincere Company in Shanghai since the spring, for the past two months. The content of his lectures is divided into thirteen lectures on Chinese history and geography. His ninth lecture will be held on Sunday afternoon at 3:00 PM. The title of the lecture is "The Seventh Unification and Expansion of Qing China." The lecture will outline the origins of Manchuria and its situation before entering the Pass, the rise of the Qing Dynasty and its unification of China, the prosperity of the Qing Dynasty's literary and military achievements, the missionary cases and the Taiping Rebellion, the intrusion of Western powers, the decline of the late Qing government, the reformist constitutionalism and revolutionary movements, and the establishment of the Republic of China. If you wish to listen to Mr. Jiang's great theories, please arrive early.

Xinhua Art School Holds Exhibition of Calligraphy by Master Hongyi

Master Hongyi's original name was Li Shutong. He was an artist of our generation. His calligraphy directly pursues the styles of the Pu and Tang dynasties. After becoming a monk, his works have become even more cherished by the world. His disciple Liu Zhiping has collected hundreds of Master Hongyi's calligraphy works over the past twenty years. They will be publicly exhibited at the Xinhua Art School in Dapuqiao, Xie Xu Road, in this city from 9:00 AM to 6:00 PM on Sunday, the 19th of this month. Admission is free.

30,000-Meter Relay Race to Be Held This Morning, Eleven Teams Participating, with Yi Bing Jia the Strongest

The 30,000-meter Jiangwan long-distance relay race, organized by the Jingwu Athletic Association, will commence at 10:00 AM this morning. Names will be called at Hongkou Park first. Then the athletes for the second, third, and fourth legs will be sent to the starting points of their respective legs. At 10:30 AM, the race will start from Hongkou Park. The entire course is 23,628 meters. A total of eleven teams will participate, among which Team Yi Bing Jia is considered the strongest. Details are as follows:

Full Course Route: 1st Leg: Starting from the west gate of Hongkou Park, passing the swimming pool, turning into East Sports Association Road, entering Xiangyin Road, to the intersection of Songhu Road, a total of 5,000 meters. 2nd Leg: From the intersection of Xiangyin Road and Songhu Road straight to Jungong Road, turning to the Water and Electricity Plant, a total of 7,480 meters. 3rd Leg: Entering Zha Yin Road to Songhu Road, turning back to Xiangyin Road, a total of 4,228 meters. 4th Leg: From the intersection of Songhu Road and Xiang Gu Road straight to Jiangwan Road, back to Hongkou Park, entering the west gate to the flower hall finish line, a total of 4,920 meters. After the athletes start running, they do not need to carry heavy coats. The coats can be worn in turn by the athletes of each leg. For example, after the athlete of the first leg reaches the finish line, they can wear the coat of the second leg athlete. Referees please arrive at the venue by 9:30 AM.

Team Rosters: Yi Bing Jia: Wang Zhenglin, Ling Xuewen, Zhang Liang, Wu Wenlin. Yi Bing Yi: Xu Yaoming, Tang Xianlin, Yu Jisheng, Li Songping. Yi Bing Bing: Guan Youwen, Wu Xuecheng, Qian Zenglong, Meng Yiliang. Hongkou Jia: Wan Yusheng, Wang Rulin, Chen Zhiming, Jin Zhaosheng. International Five-Team Track and Field Meet: Baihong Wins Championship

British Army Lancashire Second with 35 Points

Major Players Absent Yesterday, Wet Field Resulting in Mediocre Performances

The International Five-Team Track and Field Meet, organized by Haiqing, was held at Beidang Bimei Zhang Gong School in the rain yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. About two to three hundred spectators attended, so it was not too deserted. However, Baihong's Fu Baolu, Sun Huipei, Zhonghua's Wang He, Wang Zhenglin, Zhang Jiakui, etc. were absent from yesterday's competition, and the wet and muddy ground after the rain greatly affected the results. Overall, the biggest achievement of yesterday's competition was Lancashire's Bowen's 220-yard performance (23.4 seconds, breaking the old record). Wang Xuewu's javelin and Jiang Huai's triple jump performances were also considered excellent. The overall result was that the Baihong team scored 67 points, winning first place. Lancashire scored 35 points, winning second place. Xilian scored 34 points, placing third. Zhonghua scored 19 points, ranking fourth. Mailing scored 10 points, coming in last. Detailed information is recorded below.

Team Totals

First: Baihong, 67 points. Second: Lancashire, 35 points.

Third: Xilian, 34 points. Fourth: Zhonghua, 19 points.

Fifth: Mailing, 10 points.

Track Race Overview

100 Yards: In this competition, the Hua team's Luo Ye and Ma Yi made it to the preliminary rounds. Luo Ping started the fastest. Ye Li showed his power in the middle. Weller gained the championship due to his strong final sprint. Gou Lun ranked second. Zhonghua's Le Li, Fa Luo Ping swept the back two spots.

220 Yards: Zhu Guangzhi started the fastest. Tall Bowen followed closely behind. After five or six yards, Lancashire's Bowen showed his skills, taking the lead. The result was 23.4 seconds, breaking the old record.

440 Yards: Ten people started. Famous player Dai Shuguo drew the innermost lane. At the sound of the gun, Dai Shuguo, Ma Changxian, and Qiaodun closely followed. Ford and Yang Nasi fell far behind. Because no one competed with him, Dai reached the finish line with a time of 55.2 seconds. Due to the wet field, the results were mediocre.

880 Yards: Baihong's famous player Jia Lianren did not participate. Lancashire's McDonald started first. Le Junchang closely followed. After 300 yards, Le Junchang overtook Mai Cengna, striding forward. However, in the last 100 yards, Le Junchang was exhausted. Mai Funa seized the opportunity, winning over Le Junchang by five yards.

One Mile: A total of thirteen people started this race. Xilian's veteran Xu Da released a kite, eventually failing. Lu Jinming took the lead by far, running more and more bravely, 30 yards away from second-place Hall. In the last lap, Lu's pace was relaxed, his attitude calm. He reached the finish line in four minutes and fifty-one seconds. Second place was Lancashire's Hale, more than ten yards behind.

320 Yards Low Hurdles: This competition originally had two preliminary rounds, but due to a lack of half the number of people, it was temporarily changed to the final. Sun Huipei and Li Houda were absent, resulting in the championship being taken by Xilian's Sique Mi. One Mile Medley Relay: In the first leg, Baihong's Dai Shuguo gave his all, throwing off the second place by about 30 yards. When Li Houda took the baton, he also abandoned it by 30 meters. After Jia Lianren got the baton in the third leg, he let go of his feet even more. Zhonghua's Wu Wenlin also closely followed. When running to 700 yards, he was chased out by Lancashire's Like Kai. Baihong's Zhu Guangzhi took the baton in the fourth leg and reached the finish line first with a relaxed pace. Xilian won the runner-up by twenty yards later.

Field Event Overview

Pole Vault: Only Zhu Hongying, Berlin, Boliden, Bailao, and Hall jumped. Fu Baolu and Wang He were absent. Pan Berlin was the first to be eliminated. Xilian's Berlin and Lancashire's Bailao competed fiercely. When added to five feet eleven and a half inches, Bo jumped over and won the first place. Zhu Hong won the third place. Mailing Hall ranked fourth.

Triple Jump: There were no particularly exciting highlights in this competition. The top selected Jiang Huai, Cui Lianming, and five others were selected. Jiang led the crowd with forty-two feet four and a half inches in the first jump of the final. In the end, he won the body jump, adding half an inch to win first place. Cui Huang got the third and fourth, Zhonghua Hall.

Long Jump: Ten people including Balai started jumping. Zhonghua Zhang was temporarily absent. As a result of the competition, Baihong's Zhang Shenru made a big show, jumping to a score of twenty-one feet and four inches. Balai was only three and a half inches behind, winning first place. Securities: 96 Public Bonds Drop Uniquely, Gold Certificates Remain Firm and Expensive

Yesterday, the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange saw little change in market conditions, with most transactions being swaps. There was some short covering, and the trend was relatively stable. However, the 96 public bonds, which had seen no fluctuations for several weeks, suddenly declined. Most long positions exited, and there were quite a few sellers. This type of bond, which had long lost its qualification as a public bond and was勉强 (mianqiang, barely) listed among public bonds, only saw some activity from small capitalists who relied on its 利 (lì, profit). Investors naturally stayed away, and those who took long positions repeatedly failed to fabricate rumors. No one is likely to be fooled by it again, so further declines are expected. The unified public bonds, due to the 20 million still remaining in this month's deposit, had long positions concentrated in a small number of three firms, while short positions were scattered among small retail investors from various groups. The future still holds potential for change. Yesterday's session saw some short covering at the opening, with market conditions firm in the near term and weak in the distant term, fluctuating mostly by 0.05-0.10 yuan. After the yarn market declined the previous day, yesterday it presented an image of stability and tranquility. Seafood: Salmon's New Season is Approaching; Imports to Our Country

Salmon, also known as "Dong Yang Yu" (Eastern Ocean Fish), is purely soaked in nitrate, so its meat is red and its taste is very salty. It can be stored for a long time without spoiling. It is produced in the Sakhalin region bordering Japan and the Soviet Union. Every year between late summer and early autumn, new goods enter the market. It is now early summer, and fishermen from Japan and the Soviet Union are preparing to go to sea to catch them. The production volume is very large, and the number imported to our country is huge. The most popular sales locations are Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, with the rest of the country being limited. Investigations show that this type of fish has been sold in our country for less than 20 years. Before being imported to our country, it was heard that the Japanese榨 (zhà, press) the caught fish for oil, which was used as fuel or other needs. The remaining fish pressings could be used as fertilizer for irrigation. Later, Chinese seafood merchants traveling in Japan taught them the production method, and the fish became what is now known as salted fish. Initially, only a small number were shipped over for trial sales. Who knew that its taste would perfectly suit the palates of the people of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces? Moreover, the market price was extremely low at the time, only selling for 3-4 yuan per 100 jin, so the common people were happy to buy it. Later, sales increased daily, and imports increased steadily. The market price also gradually increased. The highest price ever sold was over 16 yuan. Today's market prices are quite average, with good goods priced at 10 yuan and ordinary goods priced at 9.80 yuan.

Moreover, in the past half month, the raw materials have also been procured by the Hankou groups, so the Shanghai shops' intention to sell sesame oil is firm. Therefore, the weekly price was raised to 28.30 yuan. Yesterday, the Hong Kong groups suddenly inquired and transacted over 100 tan of Bengbu goods, totaling 300 cans, so sentiment was even better. The market immediately increased to 29 yuan. If sales from various routes continue to move, the market will inevitably change for the better.

Shen Bao Children's Special

Which Path Should Children Take?

— Zhang Zhaohe

In our childhood, we are preparing to enter society and seek a fulfilling life. Therefore, we must exhibit "sincerity" in everything we do and avoid any trace of "hypocrisy." The civics course in school teaches us this every day, helping us to cultivate a good character. Recently, society has been filled with darkness, and people's hearts are becoming more treacherous day by day. Children are affected by the entanglement of negative environments and the influence of harmful trends, which inevitably impacts our individual personalities.

"Sincerity" is the expression of innate goodness. Actions that are not self-deceptive or deceptive to others easily gain people's sympathy and support. It will be much easier to serve society in the future!

"Hypocrisy" is saying one thing and meaning another, not living up to one's words, and seeking immediate gains. Once exposed, one will be scorned and reviled, with no place in society. It poses a great danger to one's future life.

From this perspective, the two paths of "sincerity" and "hypocrisy" must be clearly recognized and decisively chosen. We must know which path to take and which path to avoid. Dear and lively children, please choose carefully!

Yue Fei's Childhood

— Ning Ziqiang

Children! When we talk about national heroes, Yue Fei is considered "second to none." During the Southern Song Dynasty, there were internal and external troubles, similar to the present situation. At that time, Yue Fei did not hesitate to sacrifice himself and waged war against the Jurchen Kingdom, achieving victory after victory, like a hot knife through butter. Unexpectedly, a treacherous minister named Qin Hui appeared in the court, ordering him to withdraw his troops and plotting his death, resulting in "failure just before success," which is truly regrettable. Ah! Enough digression, let's get back to the main topic and talk about his childhood.

Yue Fei was from Tangyin County, Henan Province. He lost his father at a young age and relied on his mother's needlework to support him. From a young age, Yue Fei received his mother's teachings and deeply understood righteousness. His mother tattooed "Serve the Country with Utmost Loyalty" on his back to show the meaning of "never forgetting forever." He also received instruction from Mr. Zhou Tong, mastering both literary and martial arts. Therefore, his ability to distinguish right from wrong, differentiate interests, and his loyalty to the emperor and love for the country, leading him to die for his country on the battlefield, came from his mother's teachings. As for his superb martial arts and strategic expertise, they were due to Mr. Zhou Tong's "patient instruction." Children! Our country's current environment is much worse than that of the Southern Song Dynasty. Everyone should learn from Yue Fei's loyalty to the country!

Introducing the Children's Correspondence Club

— Ba Ling

Mr. Ayrton said, "The twentieth century is the century of children." If we carefully consider Mr. Ayrton's words, we will find them to be very profound. Precisely because the twentieth century is the century of children, we should earnestly seek happiness for children and plan for all aspects of their lives in this century. Only then can we be said to be respecting the roots of the nation.

In the past, the Shanghai Yu Tang People's Education Center organized a "Little Teacher's League" to train little teachers. Now, to further train children's communication skills, it has organized a Children's Correspondence Club. The purpose of the club is to facilitate communication among children and to enhance their ability to express themselves in writing. The method of communication is divided into group and individual communication. The content of the communication focuses on children's lives, with written language as the main body and pictures and photos as supplements. The communication time is tentatively set for once a week. The exchange of letters will be the responsibility of the instructor, who will collect and distribute them every Monday. The club also has a postmaster who is responsible for receiving and sending letters. The stationery used for children's correspondence will be based on domestic-made envelopes and stationery. For internal communication, the stationery will be printed by the general office, and the envelopes will be made by the children in the handicrafts department. For communication with little teachers outside the club, the stationery and envelopes will be distributed by the Education Center to ensure uniformity. All exchanges of letters will be kept by designated personnel. Excellent letters will be published for observation and learning. These are the measures taken by the Children's Correspondence Club. I think it is a very good organization for training children. I hope that educational institutions in various places will follow suit so that children's interest in life can be greatly enhanced.

Song of Spring Outing

— Jin Hao

In the spring of 1934, when I was in Yichang, I often went to the mountains alone to watch people worship their ancestors and sweep tombs. Inadvertently, I heard a beggar singing a short song, which I found very meaningful. Now I write it down for the enjoyment of fellow enthusiasts:

Spring outing, spring outing, everyone treads,

Trampling on the green grass at will.

What does trampling on grass matter?

There is plenty in the world before your eyes!

The rich will bully the poor,

The strong will kill the weak!

The Relationship Between Plants, Animals, and Humans

— You Mojun

Since we are human beings, we all know that clothing, food, housing, and transportation are essential to our daily lives. Although the scope of clothing, food, housing, and transportation is very broad, we must rely on the living things around us, that is, plants and animals, to meet these four needs. The relationship between plants and animals and us humans is briefly described below:

First, let's talk about clothing. In the cold weather, we need to wear fur coats, which are taken from animals. All wool products cannot be made without animals such as alpacas. Silk fabrics, as everyone knows, rely on silkworms, and silkworms are also animals. Cotton can keep us warm, and cotton yarn can be used to weave cloth. In summer, we often wear linen clothes, which all depend on plants.

Next, let's talk about food. Animal meat, such as beef and pork; eggs, such as chicken eggs and duck eggs; milk, such as cow milk and goat milk; what we eat every day, what doesn't rely on animals? Rice and wheat are our main foods, which belong to the cereal family. Soybeans and peas belong to the legume family; they can be cooked and eaten, or oil can be extracted. Oranges and bananas belong to the fruit category. Moreover, there are countless vegetables. Even our favorite products, such as tea, wine, and cigarettes, what doesn't have a relationship with plants?

Let's talk about housing again. The raw material for building houses is wood. Furniture such as tables and chairs are also made of wood. As for fuels like firewood and charcoal, what isn't wood? Therefore, without plants, our housing problem cannot be solved. Moreover, forests can also prevent floods.

Finally, let's talk about transportation. Camels, horses, and cattle can be used for transportation or to serve us, such as plowing fields and carrying heavy loads. This shows that animals have a great relationship with our transportation. The coal and oil needed for steam engines and gasoline engines are originally ancient organisms; this is another example. Plants, such as utility poles and railway sleepers, are all made of wood and are also related to human "transportation."

From the above, children can understand the relationship between plants, animals, and humans.

Ten Minutes of Science Teaching

— Bai Tao

The Hot Trick

Everything mysterious in the world has its own laws. For example, let's take boiling water as an example. It is also based on certain laws: If we put the fire on top of the pot, it will never boil. That is because when the water gets hot, it expands and becomes lighter and rises, while the cold water sinks because it is heavier. Therefore, cold water and hot water convect up and down. Eventually, all the water in the pot will be heated. At the same time, air is also like water. When the air gets hot, it also expands and becomes lighter and rises, while the cold, heavy air sinks. For example, we use a thick piece of paper and draw circles on it. Then, use scissors to cut along the circles all the way to the center of the circle, and you will have a paper circle. Tie a thread to the center of the paper circle. Then, light a candle. Put the paper circle over the candle flame, and the paper circle will rotate. This is a very interesting trick. This trick tells us that the air above the candle flame, because it is heated, expands and becomes lighter and rises. This rising air is actually a hot wind. The hot wind blows on the paper circle, and the paper circle rotates.

The diagram above shows that the hot air in the stove rises; the diagram below shows that the cold air sliding over the ice falls.

When a fire is lit in the stove, the air in the stove is heated. The hot air rises and, when it rises to the wall of the pot, it transfers the heat to the wall of the pot, and the wall of the pot transfers the heat to the water, and the water heats up. We can also play a trick to prove that hot air rises. This diagram shows that the paper circle above the flame rotates because it is pushed by the rising hot air.

Hot air rises. Therefore, the stove is placed below, and the top is hot. But cold air is not like that. Cold air is heavier, so it sinks. For example, if you eat ice cream or shaved ice in the summer. If you want the water to cool down quickly, you should put the ice on top of the cup, not below. Housewives and restaurant chefs often put the ice in the top compartment of the refrigerator and put fish, meat, milk, and fruit…etc. below. This is the reason. Because the cold air that has slid over the ice sinks because it is cold and flows over the food, so the food is cold too.

The Road is Not a Place to Play

— Chonglou

The day before yesterday, I was walking on the road and saw many children playing there. This made me think of a sentence about our country in a Soviet textbook.

The Soviet textbook once described our country simply like this: "It is a country that used to be very strong but is now weak. The most obvious symptom is that many farmers no longer farm the land and go to the city to pull rickshaws! Many children are out of school and playing on the road!" How heartbreaking this is for the people of our country, especially "children are out of school and playing on the road." Although there are many children in our country who are not out of school and do not play on the road, we can often see many children who are out of school and playing on the road.

Two Types of Children

Such a symptom cannot be entirely blamed on the children. Why not give them education? Why not give them a formal place to play?

However, I would also like to advise the children playing on the road: If your parents are poor, you should also study on your own, because playing on the road not only wastes time but is also very dangerous for your life.

What Kind of Person Will I Be in the Future?

— Guo Chengzhi, Minglun Hall Elementary School, She County

(Twelfth Place)

The loss of the Northeast, as well as the North China Incident, has shocked the people of the whole country; even countries all over the world are paying close attention to these events.

How did these things happen? To put it simply, it is because China is full of dependence and seeks temporary peace, gradually losing its self-confidence, that it has suffered the oppression and aggression of □□ imperialism.

At this critical moment for the survival of the entire nation, if we want to seek a way out for ourselves, we must first seek a way out for the nation. Therefore, what our country needs most at this time is talents with scientific minds and military knowledge.

My ambition is to be a soldier who saves the country in the future; therefore, I am very happy to participate in and pay special attention to the scout training at our school.

Being a soldier! It is not like the warlords of the Northern Warlords of our country in the past, who used to bully the people and commit various illegal acts in peacetime. Such warlords can be said to be parasites of the country and public enemies of the people.

Only in this way can I seek happiness for my country and win glory for my nation! That is also how I personally have obtained a bright road.

Everyday Science

Why Can Real Subsidiary Coins Be Picked Up by a Magnet?

— Ren

Now we have new copper coins and new jiao coins (collectively called new subsidiary coins). Children, have you seen them? These new subsidiary coins are divided into five types:

Half a cent (copper) One cent (copper)

Five cents (nickel) Ten cents (nickel)

Twenty cents (nickel)

One cent of the new subsidiary coin is equal to 30 old cash (that is, three copper coins from the Great Qing Dynasty or old national flag copper coins). According to this calculation, half a cent is equal to 15 cash; five cents is equal to 150 cash; ten cents is equal to 300 cash; twenty cents is equal to 600 cash.

Ten cents of the new subsidiary coin is equal to one jiao of paper money; twenty cents is equal to two jiao of paper money.

The new subsidiary coins are decimal: ten cents are equal to one jiao; ten jiao are equal to one yuan. (It used to be one silver dollar. Now paper money is used instead, and silver dollars are not allowed.) This decimal currency system is much more convenient and regular than the previous chaotic currency system—the previous subsidiary coins were divided into small foreign coins and big foreign coins; jiao coins also had more than ten names such as "medicine water jiao," "lead plate jiao," "private plate jiao," "Guang jiao," and "Jiangnan," which really made people dizzy!

Since the new subsidiary coins were introduced, people all over our country have found them very convenient to use.

However, where there is real, there is fake. Fake ten-cent and twenty-cent coins have now appeared on the market. Their patterns and sizes are exactly the same as the real ones, but the color is not as good as the real ones: the differences between real and fake subsidiary coins are as follows:

Fake: Grayish white, not shiny, soft, leaves a tooth mark when bitten hard;

Real: White as silver, shiny, hard, leaves no tooth mark when bitten hard.

Fake subsidiary coins are made of lead, and real subsidiary coins are made of nickel. We also have an easiest way to distinguish them: use a magnet to pick them up. Fake coins cannot be picked up, but real coins can be picked up. Because nickel is magnetic, it will attract a magnet.

The Tale of the Righteous Dog (15)

— Xin Qing

They did not refuse or deny it, but received him respectfully. The villagers gathered around, looking at him and whispering to each other, saying, "Don't you see him? He is the king of men, he is a great artist, the whole world mentions his name; yet he is just our poor little Nanluo, who used to be like a little beggar, relying on his dog to help him, exchanging bread and rice every day."

He thought about how he would put the fur coat and purple robe on his old grandfather and paint a portrait of him, like a saint in St. Clement's Church. He would also put a gold collar around Buddy's neck, place him on his grandfather's right, and then say to the people, "This is my only friend in the past." He would also build himself a white marble palace and a magnificent garden, from the slope of which one could see the spire of the Great Cathedral. He himself would not live in it, but would openly allow young people with great ambitions and no means to live there. When they praised him, he would say to them, "No, don't thank me—just thank the human painter Rubens. If it weren't for his masterpiece encouraging me, I wouldn't be where I am today."

He lived his life happily with these beautiful and impossible dreams, without any selfish ideas, and with the ambition of worshiping heroes—he was as happy as ever on Little Elo's naming day, returning to his dark hut with Buddy to eat their black bread, while all the children in the village were singing and laughing in the mill, eating round cakes and almond gingerbread. Under the starry sky and in the soft sound of flutes and harps, his companions danced in the large barn.

"It doesn't matter, Buddy, it doesn't matter, someday everything will change." He said this to Buddy, hugging the dog's neck with his arms, and sitting together at the door of the small hut, the cheerful laughter and music from the mill blowing over in the night wind.

From then on, Buddy often growled and showed his dissatisfaction whenever he walked past Corgan.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Amateur Weekly

Overseas Correspondence Network

A Country Without Women

— Cheng Zi

Thessalonica, Greece Correspondence

A country without women – that must be a strange novel depicted by a dreamer. However, no matter how skeptical you may be, there is indeed such a country on Earth. And this land has been preserved from a thousand years ago until now. Although it has made no contribution to the world, it has long occupied a portion of the Earth's surface.

What's even stranger is that there are not only no human females here, but also no female animals. Naturally, there are chickens, sheep, and cows here, and they are the same shape as chickens, sheep, and cows elsewhere, but there is not a single hen, not a single ewe, and not a single cow – they are all male.

This country without women is not in heaven or underground; it is in our real world, eighty miles from Thessaloniki, Greece, south of the Athos Peninsula protruding into the Aegean Sea, at the foot of Mount Athos, which reaches a height of six thousand feet. A total of four thousand people live in this place, all men, of course, without a single woman. These men are not allowed to cut their hair, so here you can only see long hair and beards, and no bald heads. Of course, you can't see slicked-back, wavy modern hairstyles either. At the same time, in this wonderful place, all games, songs, dances, love, and even bathing and noise are prohibited.

On the cliffs of the Athos Peninsula, there are twenty lonely isolated houses, like birds' nests, each about a mile or two apart. These isolated houses are monasteries built around the year 900 AD, and are extremely magnificent high-rise buildings. In the middle of these are also schools, churches, and fortresses. The four thousand men of the so-called country without women live here.

If there were only no women among the many monks, it would not be surprising. What is particularly interesting is that in this country without women, there are many phenomena rarely seen or even imagined by people. For example, ordinary monks in monasteries that we know of live in a certain country and have close ties with everything there, even though they claim to have seen through the mortal world. However, this country without women, although within Greece, is an independent country. Moreover, this country also has its capital, called Karyes. In this city, there are also gardens, the sound of church bells, and oxen grazing in pastures. At the same time, there are schools, shops, restaurants, banks, and post offices, but you can't see a woman in any corner.

The department stores in Karyes, the capital of the country without women, are, of course, almost the same as what we usually see, with only one difference: you can't see any of the bright-eyed, white-toothed female shop assistants that we see in general department stores here; all those who greet customers are men with long hair and beards. Naturally, there are no high-heeled shoes or anything else that women need in this store.

Everyone knows that without women, there are no men, just as without men, there will be no women. Based on this common-sense reasoning, we can know that the men of the country without women are not born in this country but come from elsewhere. Although there are many reasons for these men becoming citizens of this country, most of them come here because of the troubles of women, because of unemployment, to seek spiritual comfort, or to escape punishment. Because these people are determined to end their lives here, they only pray and read the Bible sincerely from morning to night. In fact, it seems that there is nothing else to do.

This place is on the Aegean coast, and the cold sea breeze blows for a long time, so the winter is very long. But the people here still pray from morning to night even under the biting north wind and heavy snow. Therefore, in this country without women, you can always only hear the sound of church bells and religious singing. Other than that, it is a silent world of death.

The most sacred, oldest, and most powerful monastery in the country without women is called the Lavra Monastery. On the eve of Christmas, countless candles are lit in the chapel of this ancient monastery, shining more brightly than electric lights. All the monks come to participate in this solemn ancient Christmas ceremony. At the beginning of this ancient ceremony, two acolytes dressed in gorgeous priestly robes reverently brought out the Gospel book, decorated with gold and pearls, from fourteen hundred years ago. Then, the white-haired archbishop, wearing a gold and purple robe used for ten centuries, solemnly opened the Gospel book and began to chant hymns. The monks in the hall followed with continuous prayers, shouting in unison: "Lord have mercy on us." Thus, the ceremony reached its climax.

The monks here who live for prayer have, of course, forgotten women and all material pleasures. They drink barley soup, black bread, and salted fish. They get up at two o'clock every morning to work and worship in the cold wind. As for all their habits, they are unchanging until death, just as the monks of a thousand years ago did not bathe, and the same is true now. However, strangely enough, they rarely get sick, perhaps because of their carefree and thoughtless lives.

It is not easy for outsiders to come to this country without women. They have to get permission from the local authorities. As for women, they are absolutely forbidden to enter. Therefore, if women want to visit here, they have to cleverly disguise themselves as men. If several people come here at the same time, they will be subject to strict surveillance, because the people here are most afraid of women disguising themselves and sneaking into their country without women, and even more afraid of men and women coming in together and making love and performing frivolous comedies on this "holy land," which would "contaminate" them.

It is said that one winter, two Germans came here. Because of the snowfall, they were trapped in the monastery and could not leave for a while. Their wives, who were waiting near the border, became anxious and immediately hired a motorboat, crossed the sea, entered this country without women, and frantically sounded the siren to find their husbands. Although the sound of the siren attracted the two Germans, it also attracted the attention of the monks here, who chased after the two Germans in unison, shouting: "Expel the demons! Beat them!" A thunderclap, like an earthquake, shook Mount Athos.

In 1916, because the Queen of Romania came to the Athos Peninsula, the monks here also believed that

Page 18

the holy land had been defiled. As a result, they constantly prayed for seven days and seven nights to atone for their sins!

In recent years, it is said that three Danes came to the country without women with proper permits. Among them, one, although dressed as a man, had a somewhat effeminate posture. Therefore, the monks were uneasy and gave him strict surveillance and secretly tried to examine him, but in the end, they still did not understand the truth. In this way, a big storm arose in the country without women. All four thousand monks talked about this issue. You said I was wrong, I said you were mistaken, and the situation was extremely serious, like a political dispute in an ordinary country.

Science Tidbits

— Seeking Truth

Electron Telescope

Recently, Dr. Zolkin of the American Telephone Association discovered an electron telescope that can clearly see objects in the dark. Based on the principle of Television (a device that can see distant objects by means of radio waves), it can transform invisible forms into visible forms, and can transform the invisible rays (dark lines or infrared rays) emitted by objects into visible rays. The discovery of such an electron telescope is, needless to say, a great contribution to science. With it, steamships and airplanes can travel in fog or at night, and bacteria that cannot be seen by ordinary light can be studied. Of course, it can also be used in military affairs. According to recent news, this electron telescope is also actually being used in photography.

Exploration of the Stratosphere

On November 11th of last year, the American Geographical Society and the Army Air Corps jointly planned an exploration of the stratosphere. As a result, the explorers, aboard the world's largest balloon, the Explorer II, reached a height of 72,395 feet (22,066 meters), setting a new world record for stratosphere exploration.

According to the explorers, the sunlight in the high altitude is stronger than on the ground. If you look directly at the sunlight through the window, it is simply unbearable for the eyes. However, the temperature is very low and the cold is biting, which is equally difficult to endure. If you look down at the ground from the high altitude of the stratosphere, it is completely a brown earth and a circular space. People and all living things are, of course, invisible. All that can be seen are mountains undulating like the waves of the ocean, huge rivers and lakes, which are especially clear when the sunlight is reflected. Looking up at the sky, it is a vast black world, and nothing can be seen.

The explorers in the balloon flying high into the stratosphere could talk to the ground by telephone, so everything they encountered in the air could be immediately known on the ground. At the same time, in their exploration, various scientific experiments were also carried out. Therefore, they could not only know more about the situation in the air, but also obtain many scientific experimental knowledge. For example, this American exploration brought many microorganisms from the ground to the stratosphere. As a result, many of these organisms died, and some were still alive, which is of great significance to biological research.

According to the prediction of this group of explorers, in the future, with more thorough preparation for exploring the stratosphere, they can at least rise to 95,000 feet. Indeed, mankind's knowledge of the secrets of nature and its skills in conquering nature will show even greater progress.

Ancient Creatures of the Gobi Desert

Everyone knows that the desolate desert area is not suitable for the survival of humans or even living things. However, since the existence of the earth, have there been living things in the current desert area? And has there been any cultural existence? This question is still under study.

Recently, due to the progress of science and the activity of explorers, the mysterious places that our ancestors could not reach in the past can now be explored by us, and many accurate knowledge materials can be obtained from this exploration to help scientific research and make it develop further. The desert area was also an unknown mystery in the past, but modern science has many reliable studies and discoveries about the desert, so that we can increasingly understand everything about it. What I want to say here is that there have been new and interesting discoveries in the Gobi Desert recently. This discovery is of great significance in both history and science.

As everyone knows, the Gobi Desert is a branch of the Great Gobi Desert. There have always been many explorers to this place, and there have been many discoveries, but it can be said that great achievements have not yet been seen. Recently, Mr. Osborne, the curator of the American Museum, organized an expedition to explore the Gobi Desert. As a result, he discovered some fossils of giant beasts that lived millions of years ago, which aroused great attention from general experts. At the same time, several Swedish geologists also discovered fossils of poplar and elm leaves from the geology of millions of years ago. These plants are similar to those in present-day Central Asia, and this type of fossil is especially common in the east of the Gobi Desert. At the same time, there are many similar fossils in the Mojave Desert of California and other places. Due to these facts, Mr. Osborne, the curator of the American Museum, made the following statement based on his discovery:

Perhaps this place was a swamp at that time; the giant beasts that lived here centuries ago probably survived by eating those plants.

Why did these giant beasts all die out? This is probably because the swamps in this place dried up, the plants withered, and they starved to death.

World Oddities

— Liang

Four-Eyed Fish

The fish that are usually seen only have two eyes, but the American Museum has a fish that has four eyes, so it is called a four-eyed fish.

In fact, this four-eyed fish only has two eyes. However, because the iris of its eyes is very long and divided into upper and lower parts, the upper part faces the water surface and specializes in looking at floating bait, and the lower part faces downward and specializes in looking at the water, so, on the surface and even in function, it looks like four eyes.

Rare White Animals

You have certainly seen white cranes, white horses, white sheep, etc., which is not surprising, but you have probably never even heard of pure white apes, pure white frogs, and pure white porcupines. In fact, the New York Zoo recently acquired these three treasures. It is said that it is difficult to find one of these treasures among their millions of peers. But scientifically speaking, this is probably produced by people using genetics.
